The German government announces the postponement of foreign debt remittances

Implementation Starting July 1st 52

Banks Established After the Banking Crisis Must Still Pay

Dawes-Young Loans Agreement Temporarily Unaffected

London to Convene Creditors' Meeting

(Berlin) All kinds of debts borrowed by Germany before July 1931 have now been declared to be postponed for repayment. According to the explanation of Dr. Schacht, the President of the German National Bank, Germany's current financial position was caused by the banking crisis at that time. Debts borrowed by Germany after July 1931 will be repaid as far as possible. Schacht claimed that the National Bank had invited Germany's long-term creditors and the Bank for International Settlements to attend the creditors' meeting in London on June 13. From July 1, the remittance of Germany's foreign debt repayment will be postponed. The order will be available approximately tomorrow. According to this postponement clause, the Dawes and Young loans will all be temporarily suspended for repayment, and the existing agreement will not be affected for the time being. However, Schacht hopes to find a way to reduce the burden for Germany during negotiations in London next week. The so-called remittance postponement does not mean stopping the repayment of principal and interest in marks, but only stopping the repayment in foreign currencies. German private debtors must pay into a special exchange fund managed by the National Bank. The National Bank promises to exchange marks for foreign currencies when all foreign currencies in Germany are sufficient. Bank rediscount gold debts, totaling US$46 million, will mature in July, and will now be paid in advance in US dollar bills. In this way, Germany can obtain a surplus of 30 million marks at the current dollar price. The amount of German debt affected by this postponement, calculated in British currency, is about £86.5 million. The principal and interest of this debt cannot be remitted. (Reuters, 8th)

(Berlin) Although the provisions for the suspension of debt payments have been notified by the cabinet last night, their publication will have to wait until Friday or Saturday. However, today, the President of the National Bank, Dr. Schacht, announced the news about this matter, stating that the suspension of payment of various foreign debts will not be implemented until July 1. The reason for setting this date is actually to allow Germany and its creditors to continue consultations with the London Conference next week, in order to accommodate the opinions of the creditors as much as possible. Schacht said that Germany's actions are those of an honorable debtor, who is wholeheartedly willing to fully repay its debts, but is unable to repay due to the unavailability of foreign currencies. This is not the fault of the German National Bank, but because all the warnings issued by Germany since 1924 regarding imprudent lending have not been heeded by various countries. Therefore, the real cause of this matter is the economic policy errors of various countries over the past fourteen years. Germany currently owes various countries private debts amounting to approximately £1 billion, half of which are short-term loans, and another £200 million have separate permanent contracts, which may not be subject to the suspension of payment. As for other creditors, they will be treated equally, that is, the holders of Dawes and Young bonds will not receive any preferential treatment. The meeting between the National Bank and the creditors has now been scheduled to be held in London on the 13th of this month. Representatives of long-term loan creditors and the Bank for International Settlements will all attend at that time. However, the outcome of this meeting cannot be determined by Germany alone, but depends on whether various countries can cooperate. (Guomin News Agency, 8th)

Stabilizing Exchange Rates: The British Example Can Be Followed 57

(London) Stabilizing exchange rates is the most important issue here, even tariffs and other issues have taken a back seat. Since the United States created the concept of a gold unit, financial experts here have said that the US plan can be combined with the British method of stabilizing exchange rates, which has already been implemented effectively, to find a suitable basis for stabilizing international exchange rates, so that the exchange markets of various countries do not differ greatly from the specified exchange rates. The British method is to establish a stabilization exchange rate fund. At the beginning of 1932, the pound exchange rate fluctuated, often rising and falling between US$3.25 and US$3.80 in ninety days, which troubled merchants. The British government allocated a stabilization exchange rate fund of £150 million, and secretly used it to manipulate the world exchange market and equalize the pound exchange rate. Before the United States abandoned the gold standard, it was very effective. Today, this fund has increased to £350 million. Therefore, financial experts say that once the currency prices of various countries are stabilized and the exchange rates are agreed upon with each other, a large international equalization exchange market fund can be established by the major countries together and entrusted to a neutral institution such as the International Bank for good use, in order to stabilize the exchange rates of various countries, curb the manipulation of speculators, and eliminate rumors and panic. (Guomin News Agency, 8th)

Qing Yannian Died of Poisoning 77

A Tragic Incident at a Japanese Respect for the Aged Society

Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, 5th In Osaka-Kobe's Uozaki, a Shangchi Society was held on the 3rd. 193 people attended, all of whom were elderly gentlemen and village councilors from the suburbs of Mikage, Sumiyoshi, Honjo, and Seido, totaling 330 people. On this day, after the meeting, all members took their lunch food back to their hometowns and distributed it to their families and neighbors, in order to express their intention to extend their lives and increase their longevity. Unexpectedly, all those who consumed the food were completely poisoned starting at 11:00 pm, suffering from abdominal pain and vomiting. Approximately thousands of people were affected, and hospitals in various towns were unable to accommodate them. Pharmacies everywhere were struggling to fill prescriptions, and the night was filled with disturbances and crying. In addition, the elderly suddenly suffered from serious illnesses and died one after another. Even those who were diagnosed and treated by doctors had a long way to go. Tanaka, the police chief, Yasui, the principal of the normal school, and others were also in critical condition. In particular, because the society used the elementary school as a venue, all the staff members from the principal down were severely poisoned. Upon hearing the news, the Hyogo Prefectural Sanitation Department, in addition to urgently sending epidemic prevention doctors to the Ting Song Ting Restaurant to seriously inspect food materials, also dispatched dozens of doctors from the Hyogo Prefectural Hospital and the Red Cross Hospital, divided into three shifts, to make every effort to provide relief.

Japan's Hamamatsu Air Squadron

Cause of Armory Explosion 78

Caused by Damp Ammunition

Remnants Still Smoldering Yesterday

Dentsu, Hamamatsu, 9th The Ministry of the Army has investigated the cause of the armory explosion at the Hamamatsu 7th Air Regiment, and has now largely clarified that it was not related to bombs dropped during transportation. Due to the impact of high humidity on the gunpowder used in the illuminating bombs in the armory, it spontaneously exploded and spread to nearby bombs and gasoline, causing the tragedy. According to the Military Affairs Bureau, the cause is currently under investigation, and there was no intrusion by outsiders, nor was it caused by bombs falling to the ground during transportation, because the safety devices of the bombs are very strict and difficult to explode. Therefore, the cause is outside the bombs. In addition, the 40 heavy and light bomber aircraft that were damaged suffered a loss of approximately 2 million yuan.

Japan United Press, Hamamatsu, 9th The fuel depot that caught fire due to the bomb explosion on the evening of the 7th has not been extinguished and continues to burn. Unexploded bombs are scattered nearby. The authorities have dispatched a large number of soldiers to collect them to avoid danger. According to the Army authorities, the number of deaths and injuries is 17, and two people are missing. 30 aircraft were damaged, and 6,000 boxes of aviation gasoline were burned. 360 houses of nearby residents were damaged.

Yan believes that saving the country still requires cutting troops. Shanxi Province has established a Military Reorganization Committee, which is doing its best to promote troop cuts. A considerable number of people have been implemented. Although the last batch has not been implemented, it will definitely be done in the future, because the country is only supporting heavy troops, wasting military spending in vain, and it is impossible to reduce expenditure without cutting troops, and it is impossible to save the poor without reducing expenditure. At the same time, both symptomatic and fundamental treatment should start with the development of industry. Recently, Chinese markets have been flooded with foreign goods, and the annual leakage is countless. If we continue to follow this path, foreigners will not use force to destroy China, and China itself will be invaded economically, and it will fall into the place of subjugation. Foreigners use commercial warfare, and they can destroy us without spending a single soldier or bullet. This kind of crisis is really terrible. Chinese people should broaden their horizons and focus on this point. Even if they suffer temporary humiliation, they will eventually have a day of revival. I (Xu said himself) came to Beiping this time for no other important task, just to visit Chairman Huang (Fu) and report on Shanxi's political affairs. Yan Xishan is still stationed in Taiyuan. The Jin army Li Fuying, Zhao Chengzhou, and other troops have temporarily retreated to Datong due to factual relations. According to general observations, Xu's visit this time should be to request instructions on the border defense issues between Jin and Sui. (7th)

Page 11

Han River Water Level Soars 84

=Water Mark at 39 Feet, Over a Foot Higher Than in the Past 20 Years=

=Xia Douyin Cables Asking for Instructions on Flood Prevention Measures=

Hankou Correspondence: After the severe flood disaster in Hubei Province twenty years ago, the people suffered greatly and became terrified at the sight of water. Since the beginning of summer this year, continuous rain has persisted for weeks, and mountain floods have erupted again. Both the Han and Xiang rivers have risen simultaneously and continue to rise rapidly. The Hankou water mark has reached 39 feet and 4 inches, more than a foot higher than the water level in the same month of the previous year. Regarding flood prevention matters, the General Headquarters had instructed the Hubei Provincial Government to follow the measures drafted by the National Economic Council. After discussion, the Provincial Government decided not to accept them and specifically sent Li Fanyi, the Director of the Construction Department, to Jiangxi to meet with Chiang Kai-shek, requesting changes. In addition, Chairman Xia Douyin sent a cable to Chiang Kai-shek to appeal and ask for instructions on everything. The original cable is recorded as follows: "Nanchang, To Chairman Chiang: Since the beginning of summer in Hubei Province, torrential rains have continued for days, and the river flow has risen sharply, even higher than the water level in the same month of the twentieth year. Recently, we received an order from your department to issue flood prevention measures for the Han River dikes drafted by the National Economic Council, stipulating that local governments should be responsible for flood prevention matters. The various engineering offices of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau will provide practical guidance and assistance. Flood prevention materials should be purchased by local governments according to actual needs. If the project is huge and the local financial resources are indeed insufficient, other governments may request the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to report to the National Economic Council and forward it to your department for verification and appropriate subsidies, etc. This is completely contrary to the principles of the flood prevention regulations promulgated by the former Water Conservancy Bureau in May of the twentieth year, and the flood prevention measures of the twenty-first year, where the dike bureau was responsible for the engineering and the funds were raised and distributed by the dike bureau. I humbly submit that after the two bureaus of water conservancy and dike engineering in this province were ordered to be abolished, the dike engineering was entirely the responsibility of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, and the local governments have no right to intervene. The local governments have no detailed knowledge of the previous construction plans and the current dangerous situations. Moreover, bandit troubles in central Hubei have just been pacified, and the vitality has not yet recovered. The county governments with dikes are busy comforting the people and urging taxes, and have no such strength and economy to bear the responsibility of flood prevention. Although there is an exception provision for appropriate subsidies if needed too much, it is necessary to request the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to report to the National Economic Council and forward it to your department for verification before it can be appropriately allocated. The exchange of official documents takes time, and I am afraid that the funds will not be approved before the dike collapses. The Jianghan Engineering Bureau is the only competent authority for dike engineering. When things come to a head, it actually shirks its responsibility to the local government and takes the position of assistance. The reasons and principles are unfair, and delays can be predicted. Looking ahead, I cannot help but shudder. This has been brought up at the meeting of this government, and it was decided that the flood prevention measures drafted by the National Economic Council are difficult to approve and publicly recommend Commissioner Li Fanyi to meet with you in person to request instructions. The record is on file. Now, Li Fanyi is being sent to present the report. The flood season has arrived, and at this critical moment, the lives of tens of millions of people are at stake. There is no room for hesitation. Therefore, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau's Qiu Zhidao and Cheng Renwu have discussed and divided the principles of the flood prevention work of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau's project teams and the local governments. All project command, surveying, layout, and supply of funds and materials are the responsibility of the various Jianghan Engineering Bureau offices. On the one hand, the provincial government selects engineering personnel familiar with the project to assist according to the project teams and is responsible for supervising local officials in handling recruitment and other local matters that should be compared. After Director Yang Silian returns to Hankou from the Xiang River, a decision will be made to proceed. In addition to ordering Commissioner Li Fanyi to follow the resolution and meet with you in person to explain the process in detail, this is respectfully telegraphed to you. If you approve of the above-mentioned agreed work principles as feasible, please instruct the National Economic Council to order compliance and clearly change the proposed flood prevention measures. Urgent requests, respectfully awaiting instructions, Hubei Provincial Government Chairman Xia Douyin. (Eighth day)"

Guangdong Provincial National Defense Construction Committee Established 85

丨Chen Jitang Appointed Chairman丨

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong provincial military authorities, considering the urgent national crisis and that Guangdong is located by the sea, and all coastal national defense fortresses must be actively organized and arranged for contingencies, issued 30 million yuan in national defense bonds, which were distributed by the Finance Department to various counties according to their level for subscription and sale. Since the issuance, the counties have been successively remitting the proceeds from the sale of national defense bonds for the purpose of repairing fortresses and adding new weapons. The Guangdong National Defense Construction Committee is responsible for arranging national defense matters in Guangdong Province. The committee consists of Chen Jitang, Yu Hanmou, Xiang Hanping, Li Yangjing, Miao Peinan, Li Jiechi, Huang Guangrui, Zhang Zhiying, Wu Fan, Zhou Zhi, Zhang Guoyuan, and others as members, with Chen Jitang as the chairman. Preparations have been underway for several months, and were finally completed at the end of last month. It was officially established on the first of this month and began operations immediately. All staff members of the committee are concurrently serving personnel drawn from various departments of the First Group Army Headquarters. Li Jiechi, the commander of Humen Fortress, was also appointed as the director of the National Defense Construction Committee Office to handle all official affairs within the committee. Regular meetings are held once a week, convened by the chairman. The committee's address is temporarily located within the First Group Army Headquarters. The budget for the committee's office expenses has been drafted, amounting to approximately 10,000 to 15,000 yuan per month. This funding is allocated from the national defense bond proceeds. Furthermore, considering that Shantou has a very long coastline and is an important port on the East River, where enemy ships frequently appear, the committee previously sent National Defense Committee members Li Jiechi, Zhang Guoyuan, Zhou Zhi, and several military specialists to inspect coastal fortresses in the Chao-Shan area to consolidate the maritime frontier. Recently, as the authorities have moved Li Yangjing's Third Army to the border of Jiangxi to suppress bandits, the Chao-Shan area has been taken over by Zhang Ruigui's Independent Second Division. Fearing that the troop strength would be insufficient, two regiments of Miao Peinan's Training Division were also transferred to Shantou to assist the Independent Second Division in arranging defenses. As for air defense, the Air Force Command was ordered to send aircraft to Sichuan for stationing at the discretion of the province to show thoroughness. (Third day)

Twenty-Second Year

New Budget Proposal for Hunan Province 86

=Political Expenses Six Months in Arrears=

=Implementing Austerity and Reducing Government Spending=

Changsha Correspondence: Due to the impact of the national crisis and rural economic bankruptcy, local revenue in Hunan Province has decreased significantly compared to previous years. The main sources supporting party and government expenses are the land tax, which can collect more than 200,000 yuan per month, and the production and sales tax, which has not yet been approved by the central government but can collect more than 300,000 yuan per month. For the past year, the provincial treasury has allocated political expenses once every ten days, with each allocation only being 10% of the amount owed. Therefore, as of the end of May, political expenses were six months in arrears, demonstrating the financial difficulties. The provincial government has decided to implement austerity and reduce government spending in the next year (i.e., the twenty-second year). Salaries will be discounted as follows: 90% for those with monthly salaries of 21 to 50 yuan, 85% for those with 51 to 100 yuan, 80% for those with 101 to 150 yuan, 75% for those with 151 to 200 yuan, 70% for those with 201 to 300 yuan, 60% for those with 301 to 400 yuan, and 50% for those with over 400 yuan. In addition to salaries, all expenses of various institutions will be reduced by 30%. It is estimated that the annual reduction will be approximately 3 to 4 million yuan. Based on this standard, the new local budget proposal for Hunan Province for the twenty-second year has been prepared. Both revenue and expenditure are 15,771,246 yuan, balancing income and expenses. The outline is recorded as follows: (1) Estimated amount of recurring revenue: Land tax 2,853,768 yuan, deed tax 450,000 yuan, business tax 750,000 yuan, house tax 206,593 yuan, boat tax 50,000 yuan, local property income 64,774 yuan, local business income 96,172 yuan, local administrative revenue 881,345 yuan, local business profit income 1,298,411 yuan, other income (including production and sales tax) 6,219,583 yuan, totaling 12,071,246 yuan. (2) Estimated amount of temporary revenue: Other income (including rice inspection fees, etc.) 1,200,000 yuan, bond income 2,500,000 yuan, totaling 3,700,000 yuan. The total recurring and temporary revenue is 15,771,246 yuan. (3) Estimated amount of recurring expenditure: Party affairs expenses 532,244 yuan, administrative expenses 1,830,583 yuan, judicial expenses 1,080,466 yuan, public security expenses 1,103,648 yuan, financial expenses 1,758,456 yuan, education and culture expenses 2,339,160 yuan, industrial expenses 348,536 yuan, transportation expenses 255,392 yuan, health expenses 153,112 yuan, construction expenses 180,594 yuan, assistance expenses 333,248 yuan, other expenses 801,490 yuan, reserve fund 46,990 yuan, totaling 11,576,527 yuan. (4) Estimated amount of temporary expenditure: Party affairs expenses 28,300 yuan, administrative expenses 210,400 yuan, judicial expenses 5,160 yuan, public security expenses 1,087,393 yuan, financial expenses 214,610 yuan, education and culture expenses 335,700 yuan, industrial expenses 115,115 yuan, transportation expenses 1,167,882 yuan, health expenses 5,000 yuan, construction expenses 124,527 yuan, assistance expenses 124,800 yuan, other expenses 788,440 yuan, totaling 4,194,719 yuan. The total recurring and temporary expenditure is 15,771,246 yuan. (Seventh day)

Liu Zhenhua Returns to Huangchuan

Dividing Routes to Encircle and Suppress the Red Bandits 87

Meeting of Generals Held on the Train to Allocate Tasks

He Chengjun Immediately Departs to Inspect the Bandit Situation in Eastern Hubei

Hankou Correspondence: Liu Zhenhua, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Region, after his public affairs in Hankou, boarded a special train on the Ping-Han Railway at 10 PM on the 8th to go north and transfer to Hanchuan to supervise the suppression. Liang Guanying, Commander-in-Chief of the 25th Route Army, Dai Minquan, Commander of the 45th Division, and Song Tiancai, Commander of the 75th Division, returned to their defense areas on the same train. Liu's bandit suppression plan has already been decided in Hankou, divided into three phases, each lasting one month, with a deadline of three months for complete eradication. The encirclement routes are divided into several routes, undertaken by ten divisions. Roughly, Liu Maoen and Li Sisuan will depart from Huangchuan Guangshan, Shangguan Yunxiang and Hao Mengling will depart from Yingshan Luotian, Wan Yaohuang will depart from Macheng Huang'an, and Dai Minquan's division will depart from Gushi Shangcheng, forming a large encirclement towards the bandits. Liu convened a meeting of various generals on the train to allocate tasks and provide instructions. Upon arrival in Huangchuan, he will issue a general attack order. He Chengjun, the Pacification Commissioner of Hubei, fearing that after Liu's general suppression, the bandits would flee into Hubei, decided to depart for eastern Hubei within days to inspect, arrange defenses, and provide guidance on local rehabilitation matters. After returning to Hankou from the eastern Hubei inspection, he will tour central Hubei. (Eighth day) Hankou Correspondence: The Xu, Kuang, He, and Kong factions of Red Bandits, taking advantage of the national army's movements, have separately harassed the provinces of Sichuan, Shaanxi, Henan, Anhui, Hubei, and Hunan, running amok like wild boars, seemingly poised to make a comeback. Currently, He's bandits are confined to a corner, and Kong's bandits are moving around to avoid confrontation, which is not too worrying. However, the Xu and Kuang factions are extremely active, attacking cities and seizing land, just like in the old days. The national army is currently deploying various routes for general suppression, and intense battles are expected to occur in the shortest possible time. Therefore, the recent situation of the Red Bandits and the lineup of the bandit suppression army are explored and recorded as follows.

Recent Trends of Various Red Bandit Factions 88

The areas recently harassed by the various Red Bandit factions are the border regions of Sichuan, Shaanxi, Henan, Anhui, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces. Xu Xiangqian's faction occupies northern Sichuan and southern Shaanxi, Kuang Jixun's faction occupies eastern Hubei, southern Henan, and western Anhui, He Long's faction occupies western Hubei, and Kong Hechong's faction and a part of Peng Dehuai's faction occupy southern Hubei, eastern Hunan, and western Jiangxi. Among them, the Xu and Kuang factions have the greatest strength. Xu's bandits returned from southern Shaanxi at the end of last month and captured Nanjiang on the 30th. Now, they are taking advantage of the victory to attack Bazhong, and the city of Ba is in imminent danger. This faction has a population of 30,000 to 40,000, with no fewer than 20,000 guns, organized into the false Fourth, Ninth, and Twenty-sixth Armies. The bandit leaders include Zhang Guoxuan, He Wei, and Ren Weizhang. Xu serves as the commander-in-chief. The bandits' plan is to penetrate deep into Sichuan and open up a new base area. Those in southern Shaanxi plan to sneak into northern Hubei and take the opportunity to contact the Kuang and He bandits. If they fail, they will all enter Sichuan. Kuang's bandits have the false Twenty-fourth, Twenty-fifth, and Twenty-eighth Armies. Kuang serves as the commander-in-chief, with Liao Rongkun, Shen Zemin, and Lv Huanxian serving as army commanders. Their strength is similar to Xu's faction. Kuang himself is now in southern Henan, and his followers are scattered in various counties in eastern Hubei, western Anhui, Shangcheng, Li'an, Huanggang, and Macheng. The so-called Kang district, Sanhekou, Shunheji, Hejiafan, Wenshusi, Xiangdian, Xianglushan, Longwangshan, Guojiahe, Dafengling, Fotashan, Dafoshan, Xiaofoshan, Denglongshan, Dongyizhou, Futianhe, Zhongguan Station, Yanjiahe, Songziguan, Changgangling, Qiting, Songbu, and various places in Qishan are all places where these bandits gather. Recently, Fuxian (i.e., Xinji) suddenly reported its fall, and the main force of the bandits is gathering there. It is said that they will launch a major attack on Qiliping, which was also an important bandit den in the past, where many guns must be hidden. The bandits' attention to this place is worrying. He's bandits number about 10,000, organized into seven or nine divisions. He himself is the commander-in-chief, with Wang Bingnan and others serving as division commanders. They are still in the Wufeng and Hefeng areas of western Hubei, unable to do anything due to lack of food and ammunition. Kong's bandits have the false Sixteenth, Seventeenth, and Eighteenth Armies, numbering about 10,000, with thousands of guns. The commander-in-chief is Kong himself, with Xie Weiye, Jin Bo, and others serving as division commanders, wandering in the border areas of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. Recently, they have reportedly joined forces with the false Nineteenth Army of Peng Dehuai's faction. Although they occasionally harass Xianning, Tongshan, and Yangxin counties in southern Hubei, their main force seems to be in Jiangxi. In total, the number of bandits in each faction is close to 100,000, harassing about twenty counties (in the border region). Their disturbance plans are: (1) to restore the original bandit areas, (2) to open up new bandit areas, (3) to preserve the existing bandit areas, and (4) for each faction to take contact. If they unfortunately get their wish, the consequences are unimaginable.

Deployment of Bandit Suppression Troops 89

The bandit suppression troops in various provinces, except for Tian Songyao's troops in northern Sichuan, who cannot fully resist the Xu bandits due to their participation in internal strife, are all fully deployed and will begin general suppression immediately. In eastern Hubei and southern Henan, the person in charge is Liu Zhenhua, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Region, who took office in Hankou on the 5th. The troops under his command include Chen Jicheng's First Army, Wei Lihuang's Fourteenth Army, Liu Maoen's Fifteenth Army, Wan Yaohuang's Thirteenth Division, Peng Zhenshan's Thirtieth Division, Zhang Yinxiang's Thirty-first Division, Liang Guanying's Thirty-second Division, Dai Minquan's Forty-fifth Division, Shangguan Yunxiang's Forty-seventh Division, Hao Mengling's Fifty-fourth Division, Song Tiancai's Seventy-fifth Division, Li Sisuan's Eightieth Division, and Tang Enbo's Eighty-ninth Division, totaling more than 100,000 troops, stationed in Shangcheng, Gushi, Guangshan, Luoshan, Xinyang, Hanchuan, Huang'an, Macheng, Yingshan, and Luotian counties, forming a large encirclement towards the bandits. The General Headquarters is located in Huangchuan, where Liu is stationed. Chen Jicheng and Wei Lihuang are stationed in Huangchuan and Hekou, respectively, supervising the suppression. Liu gathered Wei Lihuang, Shangguan Yunxiang, Liang Guanying, Song Tiancai, Dai Minquan, and other generals in Hankou, and a border region bandit suppression meeting was scheduled to be held on the 6th. That morning, Liu went to the headquarters to visit Chief of Staff Cao Haosen to discuss military salaries. At noon, he accompanied Wei and Shangguan to the Pacification Commissioner's Office to visit Director He Chengjun for a confidential two-hour discussion on the final preparations for bandit suppression. He then convened various generals to give instructions, ordering them to return to their defenses within days. The border region bandit suppression meeting was therefore canceled. Liu decided to go to Huangchuan on the 8th or 9th to preside over everything. In western Hubei, Xu Yuanquan is in charge of the suppression, with the entire 48th Division, Zhang Wanxin's part of the 34th Division, Zhang Gang's security team, Jiang Zuojun's New Third Brigade, and a part of Liu Jianxu's Hunan army also deployed separately, advancing towards the Shihe bandit den. Xu departed from Shashi on the 6th to inspect Yichang and then transferred to the front to command. In southern Hubei and eastern Hunan, He Jian is in charge of the suppression, and in addition to the remaining Fourth Route Army, the divisions of Guo Rudong and Feng Yuxian stationed in southern Hubei are also under his command. The two divisions of the Fourth Route Army, Tao Guang and Wang Dongyuan, have now entered Jiangxi, and the air squadron has also departed for reconnaissance. Guo's division, Feng's division, and the divisions of Xie Bin and Rong Jingfang are stationed in Daye, Yangxin, Chongyang, Tongshan, and Xianning in Hubei. He Jian himself will be stationed in Pingxiang within days. The total number of national army troops is no fewer than twenty divisions, and all are elite. Once they join forces to encircle and suppress, their advance will be unstoppable. Although the bandits are cunning, they will have no way to survive.

Guangdong Province Reorganization

Provincial Guard Corps 90

Stipulating Personnel Numbers and Expenses and Recruiting Soldiers from the People

Establishing Joint Defense Command Headquartered Led by Military Agencies

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province has recently been actively organizing militia to establish local military force. All former militia, since January of this year, have had the counties establish Guard Corps Compilation Offices to engage in training. The Compilation Office is headed by a positive and vice director, the county magistrate simultaneously with the positive director, the vice director from the Pacification Office dispatched a military commissioner to serve as. Recently, in the bandit suppression period, the defense army is transferred in an irregular way, and the local self-defense force should be actively rectified in order to achieve the purpose of people's self-defense, and the county chief's government affairs are numerous and complicated, and I am afraid that the police force will not be able to concentrate on compiling and training, so the military authorities, in order to make the guard corps reach the army, have decided that every three or two counties will set up a police team joint defense headquarters, which is set up to command the military training and bandit suppression and maintain public security. The Joint Defense Headquarters will be established after the Southeast, Northwest, and Southwest Pacification Commissioners' Offices are abolished. As for the Eastern District, due to special circumstances, the Chao'an, Jieyang, and Puning Counties Joint Defense Headquarters were established first, and a certain person was appointed by the First Group Army Headquarters to serve as the Joint Defense Commander of the three counties. As for the plan to reorganize the provincial guard corps, the provincial government has also formulated it in recent days, including: (1) Drafting a phased compilation and implementation plan, estimating 5 million qualified strong men in the province, divided into 300 regular companies and 500 reserve companies, the number of companies temporarily averaged (2) The guard corps funds are provided by the provincial treasury, temporarily setting the regular team funds at 6 million yuan per year, the reserve team funds at 1 million yuan per year, and the county compilation office funds at 700,000 yuan per year, and collecting grain tax subjects from the people, and stopping all harsh taxes and middle-class malpractices, (3) Determine the highest command organ of the guard corps, such as Liu Gui directly under the provincial government, subordinate to the headquarters command, and use temporary command names to command, (According to the above, the First Group Army Headquarters has set up a county joint defense headquarters, and has appointed the Chaojie Pu three-county joint defense commander, then the county guard corps will be directly under the headquarters, which seems to have been determined,) (4) Implement a compulsory regular system, completely reform the previous recruitment methods, and recruit soldiers from the people uniformly, (5) Compile and train reserve teams in stages, organize reserve teams at the same time when organizing regular teams, set a time for rotation training, (6) Train cadres and talents, set up cadre training institutes and guard talent training institutions, (7) Strictly clarify rewards and punishments, all regular and reserve teams that have been handled effectively, or those who have not received training, or those who have not been recruited, should be rewarded and punished to encourage them. This plan will be implemented after being submitted to the provincial affairs meeting for approval. (Second day)

Wuxi

Cocoon Shops Stop Weighing, Silk Factories Resume Operations 96

The cocoon shops in the four townships of this county have been weighing for eight days, and the receipt of goods is also sparse. As of yesterday, the early cocoon shops have stopped weighing one after another, about more than 100, and there are still a few cocoon shops, because they are preparing to receive late fresh cocoons, and will extend the weighing to a week later. The purchase results of this silk factory are very good, especially because the cocoon body is good, which is very different from the past, and the reeling is very short. It is expected that the future profits will be optimistic, and the silk market is active, so the general silk merchants are happy, and are preparing to start the car one after another. Compared with the heyday of 49 silk factories, it can start about 70% of the work, but the problem of recruiting female workers is panic, because the former female workers have sought a livelihood with the silk industry's depression, and now the factory wants to recruit a large number of female workers at one time, which is not easy, and the wages are low and thin, each worker is only four corners for the high ones, and the low ones are triangular two corners, the general female workers, regardless of the joy, so the factories are also quite anxious about this, and are now trying to solve it.

Repercussions of the Public Safety Bureau's News Blockade 97

The Public Safety Bureau's affairs occupy an essential position in the news carried by local newspapers. Previous Public Safety Bureau chiefs all facilitated news reporters' interviews. Since Wu Dexin took office as the bureau chief, he had also followed established practices. However, recently, after the newly appointed Chief of the First Section of the Public Safety Bureau, Ji Nianru, arrived, he advised Director Wu that all public security matters, whether related to opium, gambling, prostitution, or theft, must be handled secretly. Any leakage must be avoided to prevent being hampered. Therefore, a news blockade policy was implemented. Yesterday afternoon, when reporters went to the Public Safety Bureau to gather news, Ji Nianru said that henceforth, news reporters would not be allowed into the Public Safety Bureau. The reporters believe that even if the Public Safety Bureau has unavoidable difficulties, it can clearly announce them. Why did this sudden decision come about? This is truly a cause for concern regarding the Public Safety Bureau's future. Subsequently, realizing that reasoning with Ji was futile, they all left and reported the matter to the Newspaper Reporters Association, requesting a general membership meeting to discuss countermeasures.

Money Exchange Businesses Request Reduction in Business Tax 100

Previously, the Shaoxing money exchange businesses found it difficult to bear the increase in business tax to 10 per mille. An explanation was given that Shanghai was a place where Chinese and foreigners lived together, thus deserving a tax reduction. The Shaoxing money exchange businesses felt dissatisfied with the unequal tax treatment for the same type of business. Yesterday, they sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, requesting it to forward their request to the Ministry of Finance for a tax reduction to alleviate their financial difficulties.

[Hangzhou]

Kidnapping Den Uncovered 101

The provincial capital's military police inspection team, while inspecting hotels in the new market last night, went to Room 103 of the Xihu Yingzhou Hotel. There, they found a man in military uniform lodging with a woman. When questioned, they gave evasive answers. The team leader, Director Wu, interrogated them and learned that the man's name was Xu Rongsheng and that he was a "Wu Chai" brother from Tiandeng Village in Xixiang, Shengxian. The woman, Chen Zhangshi, was the wife of a friend whom he claimed he was escorting to Nanjing. Unexpectedly, Chen Jincai, claiming to be Chen Zhangshi's husband, came to the team inquiring about her. Director Wu detained him. Chen confessed that he was the deputy leader of Tiandeng Village and that because they had repeatedly kidnapped and extorted ransoms in Shengxian, they had opened fire on the patrol team once on the 3rd of this month, wounding officers. He also said that they had come to Hangzhou as a gang, intending to carry out two kidnapping operations near West Lake. He also revealed that their Hangzhou base was located at No. 19 Erqiao, Menfu. Director Wu immediately led Deputy Team Leader He Jiachong to the address, where they captured three more bandits, Hua Ayan, Hua Youcai, and Zhang Jindi, as well as the house owner, Yu Apeng. All were detained and a pistol with twenty rounds of ammunition was seized. All confessed to repeatedly committing kidnapping offenses. Documents will be prepared and transferred to the martial law headquarters for interrogation.

Zhang Dianjiu, Deputy Commander of the Northeast People's Salvation Army, along with Han Liru, Director of the Heilongjiang Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, and a group of forty-two people, returned to China from Germany aboard the Sabrogan of the Maisons et Comptoirs d'Extrême-Orient. Mr. Zhang's Demeanor 107

General Zhang Dianjiu is nearly sixty years old, tall and robust, with a short, handlebar mustache that is flecked with grey. He has a kind and approachable demeanor and his spirit is vibrant. He is truly a hero who remains vigorous in his old age.

Remarks 108

The reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency met with Mr. Zhang on the ship yesterday. According to him:

When we retreated from Dolon with Chairman Ma (Zhanshan) into Russian territory, there were approximately four thousand soldiers. We stayed in the Soviet Union for a relatively long time and only stopped in Germany for a week before going to Italy. We departed from Zyata on May 1st. Due to slow travel along the way, the sea voyage took about forty days before we arrived here today. Looking back on our time in Europe, we were treated favorably by various sectors of the local communities. The troops I led, except for a portion that went to the border of Chahar, have all arrived in Xinjiang. All matters regarding the anti-Japanese war and my future actions will be subject to the orders of the Central Government and Chairman Ma. I have no personal opinions to express. After arriving in Shanghai, I will not go to Nanjing for the time being. As for Wang Delin and Kong Xianrong, although they returned on the same ship, they disembarked in Hong Kong and went to Guangdong. It is not yet known when they will come to Shanghai.

According to Ma Kui, speaking to a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency, General Zhang is scheduled to hold a reception for local reporters at the Da Zhonghua Hotel at 10:00 AM today to report on the anti-Japanese campaign.

Chief Technician of the Central Mint

Grand Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 110

The Mint's Auditing Committee Held Its Second Meeting Yesterday

New Coins Were Submitted to Various Assay Agencies for Examination

After the Central Mint began minting new coins, Chief Technician Grand arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning and immediately went to the mint to inspect the minting machinery. The Auditing Committee held its second meeting at 4:30 PM to welcome the chief technician and decided that the Standing Committee would submit the new coins to various assay agencies in Shanghai and other cities for examination. Details are as follows:

Mr. Grand's Arrival in Shanghai 111

The Central Mint hired Mr. Grand, an American minting expert, as its chief technician. He arrived on the Dalai at 8:30 AM yesterday and landed at the Xin Guan Wharf. Vice Director Wei Jingzhou of the Mint and representatives from foreign banks went to the wharf to welcome him. At 10:00 AM, he went to the Xiaoshadu Mint, where he was accompanied by Vice Director Wei Jingzhou to inspect the minting machinery. At 1:00 PM, he visited Kong Xiangxi, chairman of the Auditing Committee.

New Coin Minting Regulations 112

In accordance with the regulations for minting silver standard currency, the Central Mint is increasing its daily output of new coins to over 200,000 yuan. The minted coins are temporarily stored in the vault. After the Auditing Committee sends assayers to verify that the coins meet the legal standards for fineness and weight, they can be circulated on the market. In addition, mint bars will be produced, each bar containing 1,000 silver coins, with a fineness of .999 pure and a gross weight of 739.0774 ounces. The bars are rectangular in shape, with the Chinese and English characters for "Central Mint One Thousand Yuan Bar" on the front, along with the fineness and weight.

The New Coin Auditing Committee (Photo by Li Zunyong) 113

Auditing Meeting 114

The Auditing Committee held its second meeting at 4:30 PM yesterday at the Central Bank on the Bund. The committee members present included Kong Xiangxi, Chen Xing, Xi Demao, Li Fuson, Qian Xinzhi, Xu Jigu, Xu Xinliu, Chen Guangfu, Xie Taofu, Qin Runqing, Wu Yunzhai, Ye Fuxiao, Hu Junzhuang, Jian Dongpu, Hao Shumin, Lei Shengbo, Ma Su, Lin Shu, Ma Xier, David, Reese, Minar, Spiman, Geng Aide, Mackay, Shi Huang, Stedman, and Dai Jingfu. Those attending as observers included Lu Xuepu, director of the mint; Wei Jingzhou, vice director of the mint; and Grand, the chief technician. Absent were Bei Songsun and Zhang Gongquan.

Mr. Grand's Report 115

Chairman Kong Xiangxi reported on the purpose of the meeting and welcomed Grand, the chief technician of the mint, to report on the state of the U.S. Mint. Grand then gave a report, which was translated as follows: In the U.S. Mint, the minted coins are submitted to the Treasury Department of the Ministry of Finance for assay. A fee of one yuan is charged for every 5,000 yuan submitted for assay. After the coins are certified as qualified, they are issued for circulation. The fineness is very good. On one occasion, during an assay, a coin was found to be below the required fineness. Fortunately, it had not been issued and was reminted. Now, China stipulates that the tolerance for the weight and fineness of each silver standard coin compared to the legal weight and fineness must not exceed three per mille. This is even stricter than in the U.S. Mint. If we work hard and find ways to do things, we will surely achieve our goal. If you want to study the situation of the U.S. Mint, I am happy to answer your questions at any time.

Resolutions 116

After the discussion began: (1) The working hours of the Auditing Committee were resolved to be eight hours per day. (2) In accordance with the Auditing Regulations, one secretary will be appointed. It was resolved that this position would be temporarily filled by the Secretariat of the Central Bank. (3) One assayer will be appointed to handle assaying affairs. It was resolved that, before the appointee arrives, the newly minted coins would be submitted to various assay agencies in Shanghai and other cities for examination by the Standing Committee. (4) The draft rules of procedure were resolved to be amended and approved. (5) Matters concerning the assessment of mint operations and the auditing of accounts were resolved to be decided at the next general meeting. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Tang Youren, Chu Minyi, and Niu Yongjian took the night express train to Nanjing yesterday.

Q Q Q Q Q Expelled Sixth Batch

Displaced Chinese Refugees from Mexico Pass Through Shanghai Yesterday on Their Way Home 118

= A Total of 118 Men, Women, and Children =

= A Second Refugee Meeting Was Held at the Xin Xin Restaurant =

= Left Shanghai This Morning for Hong Kong to Return to Their Native Guangdong =

The anti-Chinese tide in Mexico continues unabated and is becoming increasingly severe. Five batches of Chinese refugees from Mexico have been expelled and returned to China, totaling over 4,000 people. At 8:30 AM yesterday morning, a sixth batch of 118 displaced Chinese refugees, including men, women, and children, arrived in Shanghai aboard the President Coolidge of the Dollar Steamship Lines. The Shanghai Global Chinese Association and the Mexican Refugee Relief Association both sent representatives to the Dollar Wharf in Pudong to provide assistance. The Xin Xin Ballroom on Nanjing Road was used as a temporary reception center. Details are as follows:

Arrival Situation 119

The President Coolidge entered the Wusongkou at 4:30 AM yesterday and docked at the

Photo of Chinese Refugees from Mexico Arriving in Shanghai (Photo by Xin Sheng News Agency) 120

Bailianjing Dollar Wharf in Pudong at 6:00 AM. The Global Chinese Association sent representatives Peng Canguang, Fang Difei, Gu Bingyan, Gao Qingzi, Xie Jianping, and Chen Hanbin, along with Refugee Relief Association representatives Huang Zhulin, Lin Wenli, Lin Qian, Lin Huangsheng, and Lin Huiyao, Zhang Baizi, and a group of twelve people, to the Dollar Wharf in Pudong from the Xin Guan Wharf by ferry at 6:00 AM yesterday morning to greet them. Huang Zhulin, on behalf of the group, explained the significance of welcoming them, and after all the refugees signed and registered, they took the ferry and arrived at the Xin Guan Wharf at 9:30 AM. The refugees all carried flags and marched in formation along the Bund and Nanjing Road to the Xin Xin Ballroom on Guizhou Road to rest. When the refugees passed through Nanjing Road, Chinese and foreign pedestrians stopped to watch and sighed incessantly.

Wretched Condition 121

After arriving at the Xin Xin Ballroom, the refugees took a group photo to commemorate the occasion. The Refugee Relief Association bought a large number of steamed buns and distributed them to the refugees to satisfy their hunger. The Global Chinese Association not only provided lunch at the Xin Xin Restaurant but also gave each person a temporary relief payment of ten yuan. Because the refugees had been expelled in a hurry, they had nothing with them except the clothes on their backs. In addition, they were physically and mentally exhausted from the long journey and were in a wretched condition.

Refugee Meeting 122

After resting briefly at the Xin Xin Ballroom, the refugees convened the second refugee meeting at the Xin Xin Restaurant at 11:00 AM. Huang Zhulin, Zhen , and Huang Zhaojun were elected as the presidium of the meeting. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded below: A. Reports: (1) Huang Zhulin, Chairman of the Mexican Chinese Refugee Relief Association, reported on the reasons for establishing the Refugee Relief Association on June 1st. (2) Huang Zhulin reported on the proceedings and resolutions of the first refugee meeting held in Shanghai on May 26th. (3) Yan Dajue, representative of the Global Chinese Association, reported that the total amount of relief donations received in May was 18,730 yuan. After deducting relief payments, the remaining funds have been transferred to the Refugee Relief Association for distribution. (4) Huang Qijia, a refugee from the sixth batch forced to return to China, reported on the latest anti-Chinese situation in Mexico. B. Discussion Items: (1) Huang Zhangjin and Xiao Zuguui, refugees from the sixth batch, jointly proposed that all refugees in the sixth batch should join the Refugee Relief Association and that Huang Chengren, Huang Zhulin, and five others from the Global Chinese Association be designated as the fully empowered representatives of the refugees. The proposal was put to a vote and passed unanimously. (2) Chairman Huang Zhulin proposed that the meeting should send a telegram to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission reporting on the circumstances of the refugees' expulsion and requesting assistance. The proposal was put to a vote and passed. (3) Refugee Wen Yao proposed that the meeting should send a telegram supporting the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission and the Shanghai Global Chinese Association. The proposal was put to a vote and passed and was referred to the Refugee Relief Association for handling. (4) Refugee Huang Zhangjin proposed that the Refugee Relief Association be entrusted with handling matters related to the relief of Mexican refugees. The proposal was put to a vote and passed. After the discussion, Yan Dajue, a lawyer and representative of the Global Chinese Association, delivered a speech. The meeting adjourned at 1:00 PM.

Returning Home This Morning 123

Most of the refugees who came to Shanghai this time were from Guangdong, Nanhai, Zhongshan, Taishan, and other counties. Because they had been away from their hometowns for a long time, they were eager to return home. Therefore, they did not delay their stay in Shanghai. They boarded the original ship last night to go to Hong Kong and then to Guangdong to return to their native places. The ship departed from Shanghai at 5:00 AM this morning.

Refugee Interview 124

According to Liu Sen, a refugee who came to Shanghai, speaking to a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency, the anti-Chinese sentiment in Mexico is getting worse every day. The cruelty of the situation is not only rare in China and abroad but also unprecedented in ancient and modern times. In particular, the anti-Chinese activities in the two provinces of Shunshan are the most severe in terms of insulting overseas Chinese. The party has a great influence and arbitrarily drives cars to capture overseas Chinese every day, driving them to remote mountains and cliffs and leaving them to die. In addition to privately torturing overseas Chinese, they also prevent Chinese businesses from operating and confiscate their property, which is inhumane. Although the central government of that country has ordered the authorities of the two provinces to stop this action, the provinces are autonomous and the order has no effect. Therefore, although the Chinese government has sent a protest note, it has no effect whatsoever. He expressed his indignation and hoped that the Chinese government would vigorously negotiate with the Mexican government to maintain China's prestige and protect the lives of overseas Chinese.

List of Refugees 125

The list of refugees who came to Shanghai this time is as follows: Feng Yu, Feng Sheng, Zhu Jin, Zhu's wife, Liu Ze, Mei Yu (all from Nanhai); Chen Shiyu, Chen's wife, and three children; Huang Fu, Zheng Sugong, Huang Rui, Lin You, Ou Han, Huang Lai, Liu Sen, Liang Jiu, Yu Zhen, and three children; Lin Hao, Lin's wife, five children; Li Jie, Li's wife, and three children; Li Bing, Li's wife, and four children; Peng San, Peng's wife, one child; Xiao Shuzhuang, Xiao Zugui, Peng Gu, Peng's wife and four children; Huang Jiekun, Liang Caifa, Huang Zhangjin, Huang's wife and four children (all from Zhongshan); Chen Runyan, Huang Canlin, Zhen Xin, Zhen's wife, Luo An, Huang Jinqing, Zhu Yu, Huang Zhong, Huang Zhaojun, Wen Yao, Zhen He, Zhen's wife and three children, Huang Ming, Huang Guoan (all from Taishan); Huang Chengjiu, Zhang Peixiu, Huang Qijia, Hu Fu, Wang Wenxiang, Wang's wife and one child, Tan Tian, Tan's wife and three children, Chen Liangye (all from Guanping); Lin Biji, Lin's wife and four children, Li Quan, Chen Quanhe, Chen En (all from Xinhui); Pan Cuncheng, Zheng Zheng (all from Fujian).

Telegram to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission 126

The Shanghai Global Chinese Association and the Refugee Relief Association jointly provided assistance and gave each person a relief payment of ten yuan. At noon today, the refugees convened the second refugee meeting at the Xin Xin Restaurant on Nanjing Road to discuss further actions. A motion was proposed by Zhulin to send a telegram to your esteemed commission reporting on the circumstances of the refugees' arrival in Shanghai to show respect. This proposal was recorded and is now respectfully submitted for your examination. We respectfully request that you promptly devise a way to provide relief to alleviate the refugees' distress. The New Aircraft Will Arrive at 10:00 AM This Morning

One of the Aircraft Will Remain in Lanzhou Temporarily

Two of the Junkers aircraft have been purchased, and pilots Bolt and Lutz were assigned to pilot them for a trial flight on the entire Eurasia route. The aircraft took off from Berlin on May 31st, arrived in Moscow on the 2nd, in Dihua on the 5th, and in Lanzhou on the 8th. (Invitation to Visit)

In addition to leading company employees to the airport at 9:00 AM this morning to welcome the aircraft, Li Jingzong, General Manager of the company, also sent letters to leaders in the transportation industry, inviting them to send representatives to the airport to inspect the cotton and wheat loan agreement reached between China and the United States.

Expression from the City Farmers' Association 132

Telegram Requesting Maintenance of Wheat Prices

Since the Ministry of Finance negotiated a 50 million dollar cotton and wheat loan with the United States, all sectors of this city have been paying close attention. The City Farmers' Association, due to the recent arrival of new wheat on the market and the resulting low prices which have greatly affected the lives of farmers, yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Industry to find ways to maintain prices. The original telegram is recorded below: To Chen Jun, Minister of Industry in Nanjing: We are deeply concerned about the current sharp drop in market prices of agricultural products, which is causing immense hardship for farmers. Recently, we learned that the Ministry of Finance is borrowing 50 million US dollars to purchase American cotton and wheat, and after reading this, we cannot help but be alarmed. We feel compelled to speak out to Your Excellency. Our country's agricultural products mainly consist of cotton, rice, beans, and wheat. In recent years, prices have been declining, and the situation is now even worse. Currently, the market price of wheat is only 1.9 yuan per dan (unit of weight), and barley is even less. In this time of social and economic depression, low prices are beneficial to the livelihood of the people, but the wages, fertilizers, and daily necessities required by farmers for planting have not only not decreased, but have increased daily. Now, the price of their produce is being devalued, which is unfair. Farmers cannot even recover their costs. If foreign wheat is dumped on the market, it is inevitable that the price of domestic wheat will continue to fall. The government's intention to benefit the farmers will actually harm them. We believe that this has not been carefully considered. The Association witnesses this situation and cannot remain silent. We dare to speak out, hoping that the Ministry will take effective measures to maintain the price of domestic wheat after purchasing American wheat, so as to increase the reward for farmers' hard work and rescue them from their precarious situation. This will also benefit the social economy and the lifeline of the nation. We are deeply concerned and await your instructions. Respectfully, the Shanghai City Farmers' Association.

Inspection of Enemy Goods in Two Industries 133

(Southern Goods) The Enemy Goods Inspection Committee held its fourth meeting yesterday afternoon at 2 pm to discuss active measures to eliminate enemy goods. More than twenty people attended including Lu Wenji, Huang Benli, Xu Baoqi, Huang Jiabang, and Ni Baofu. Chairman Gong Jingyan reported on the registration of various stores and the reporting of unscrupulous merchants. Then, the following resolutions were passed: (1) All stores in the city must submit their registration forms to the committee within three days. (2) On the 11th of this month, the American Settlement will be the first area to be investigated separately. (3) Comrades Yao Fenglin and Huang Jiabang were assigned to inspect a certain store on Kang Nao Road for secretly importing large quantities of enemy goods. (4) Omitted. (5) Inspectors must wear badges when working. (6) District meetings will be held to discuss the elimination of enemy goods within a specified period. The meeting adjourned after the discussions. (Silk Weaving Industry) The Shanghai Electrical Machinery and Silk Weaving Industry Association was extremely alarmed by the report in the newspaper the day before yesterday about the Nanjing telegram stating that Japanese silk was being transported to Shanghai with reduced tariffs, and that famous silk factories and fabric factories were placing orders one after another. Since this matter concerns the reputation of the entire industry and will undermine the future of domestic goods, an emergency meeting was immediately convened. It was unanimously agreed that China is a silk-producing country, and customs reports have never shown any imports of Japanese silk. Moreover, in recent years, the Chinese silk industry has been declining, and silk prices have fallen sharply, even below cost. Currently, the domestic raw silk used by Shanghai's silk factories costs an average of no more than 750 yuan per dan, while Japanese raw silk, according to yesterday's Reuters telegram, costs 980 Japanese yen per dan. Based on this situation, it is not cost-effective to transport Japanese silk to China with reduced tariffs. However, it is possible that Japanese silk merchants are intentionally dumping goods at low prices, and unscrupulous merchants are disregarding morality and secretly adopting them. Yesterday, the association believed that this matter has a great impact on China's silk industry. It is imperative to investigate the truth. Yesterday, it has already submitted a request to the Customs Superintendent and the Tax Affairs Department and sent a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce, asking them to thoroughly investigate the matter to clarify the truth.

Military Affairs Commission Replies to the Telegram from the Association to Abolish War 134

The Reorganization of Sichuan's Administration Should Be Implemented According to Principles

The Import of Military Supplies Has Long Been Explicitly Prohibited

The General Association for the Abolition of Civil War Alliance, in order to fundamentally resolve the Sichuan war, telegraphed the Military Affairs Commission in winter, requesting the rapid implementation of the predetermined principles and methods of the Executive Yuan for reorganizing Sichuan Province, and prohibiting the import of military supplies into Sichuan Province. After the telegram was sent, the Military Affairs Commission replied yesterday as follows: To the General Association for the Abolition of Civil War Alliance on Dege Port Road, Shanghai: Your winter telegram regarding the methods for reorganizing Sichuan's military and political affairs has been approved. Please implement them promptly according to the predetermined principles, and strictly enforce the ban so that no military supplies may be transported into Sichuan Province in the future, in order to stem the source of chaos and alleviate Sichuan's suffering. The methods for reorganizing Sichuan's military and political affairs should be implemented according to the predetermined principles. As for the import of military supplies, it has long been explicitly prohibited. This is a special telegram in reply for your information. Respectfully, Military Affairs Commission, Yu Zhan Seal.

Li Liejun Talks About Solidarity Against Foreign Aggression 135

The Central Government Will Adopt the Opinions of the Southwest as Much as Possible

If Ordered to Go to Guangdong, I Dare Not Refuse

According to the Central News Agency, Mr. Li Liejun of the Central Committee, accompanied by his secretary Zhang Mi Gong, arrived in Shanghai by express train at 4:50 PM yesterday afternoon after departing at 10:00 AM. He immediately returned to his residence to rest. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. Li at his residence last night to inquire about the current situation in Chahar and other issues. According to Mr. Li, he only knows about the current situation in Chahar from news reports and has no special information. As far as he knows, Mr. Feng Huanzhang's actions are entirely directed towards foreign aggression and not internal conflicts. In order to seek national unity and avoid internal divisions within the party, the Central Government has decided to postpone the convocation of the Provisional National Congress and hold the Fifth National Congress on November 12th. Although this move may seem to break faith with the people, it is by no means the responsibility of the Central Government. The Central Government has adopted the principle of "turning major issues into minor issues and minor issues into no issues" in order to seek national spiritual unity and unanimously resist foreign aggression. The Central Government has adopted the opinions of the Southwest as much as possible, and the spiritual cooperation between the Central Government and the Southwest will soon become a reality. The Central Government previously discussed sending representatives to Guangdong to explain misunderstandings, but no formal decision has been made. Several people may be sent to Guangdong within a few days, but the number and selection of personnel have not yet been determined. Generals Ma Zhanshan and Su Bingwen have already gone to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and will stay in Lushan for a short period of time for recuperation. Mr. Li himself has recently been suffering from high blood pressure and also plans to go to Kuling for a short period of time for recuperation. The reporter then asked Mr. Li whether the rumors that he would be going to Guangdong on behalf of the Central Government were true. Mr. Li replied that if the Central Government ordered him to do so, he would certainly not refuse.

Ma and Su's Arrival in Shanghai Undetermined 136

Welcome Meetings of Various Groups Postponed

Various groups in this city previously planned to hold a grand welcome for the anti-Japanese heroes Ma and Su upon their return to China and telegraphed Ma and Su to come to Shanghai. Ma and Su replied to the various groups from Nanjing yesterday, stating: "To the City Chamber of Commerce and all groups: We have received your telegram with respect. Zhanshan and others have returned to the country with guilt and deeply feel indebted. We are grateful for your previous welcome and even more grateful for your telegram invitation. However, our mission is not yet completed, and we must stay for a few more days. We plan to come to Shanghai when we have time to express our gratitude in person. Respectfully, Ma Zhanshan, Su Bingwen." It is now heard that the welcome meetings of various groups, originally scheduled to be held on the 11th, will also be postponed.

British New Warship Launched Yesterday 137

Mrs. Mougen Throws the Bottle

The shallow-water gunboat commissioned by the British Navy to be built at the Jiangnan Shipyard, known as the (Sandoiker) in Western languages, has been largely completed and held a launching ceremony at 1:00 PM yesterday. Mrs. Mougen, the chief engineer of the shipyard, threw the bottle to name the ship. More than a hundred people attended, including the British Consul-General and his wife, and important figures from the British Navy stationed in Shanghai, making it a grand occasion. The details are recorded as follows:

(Arrangement of the Ceremony Platform) The ceremony platform was located at the West Fort, with the ship surrounded by international naval signal flags. The British flag and the Chinese flag with the Blue Sky, White Sun, and a Wholly Red Earth were hung high on both sides. A bottle of champagne wrapped in a five-color silk ribbon was tied to the bow of the ship. Soldiers from the Naval Guard Battalion maintained order and security below the platform.

(Launching Order) Yesterday's launching ceremony followed the British format completely: (1) Singing hymns, (2) Playing music (by the famous Lancashire Army Band stationed in Shanghai), (3) Prayer, (4) Blessing, (5) Singing the British national anthem, (6) Naming ceremony, (7) Bottle throwing and launching, (8) Tea and refreshments.

(Chinese and Western Guests) Yesterday, guests who participated, in addition to going directly to Gaochang Temple by car, mostly took the Jiangnan small steamer provided by the shipyard from the Customs Wharf at 12:30 PM. They included the British Consul-General in Shanghai (Mr. Jaurodfn) and his wife, the chief engineer of the shipyard, Mr. Mougen and his wife, the customs inspector and the ship's supervisor (Mr. Holk Road), dozens of naval officers, the entire Lancashire Army Band, and two pastors. From the Chinese Navy, those who attended included the Deputy Director of the shipyard, Chen Zaofan (Director Chen Shaokuan was in Beijing), Lin Yuanquan, captain of the Yingrui warship, Qiu Zizhong, captain of the Ziqiang warship, Wu Shenli, staff officer of the First Fleet Headquarters, Captain Ouyang of the Hairong warship, Jiang Xihu, Captains Gan and Huang of the Jun warship, and Weng Zuguang of the shipyard's secretarial department, totaling more than a hundred people.

(Grand Bottle-Throwing Scene) At 1:10 PM, the ceremony began with a pastor leading the singing of hymns and prayers, and the Lancashire Army Band playing music. Then, the bottle-throwing ceremony was performed. Mrs. Mougen held a bouquet of flowers in her left hand and a champagne bottle tied with a five-color silk ribbon to the bow of the ship in her right hand. When the bell rang, she aimed the bottle at the bow of the ship and threw it with force. With a loud crash and champagne splattering everywhere, the ship slid into the Huangpu River amidst cheers and applause.

(Reception with Tea and Refreshments) After the bottle-throwing ceremony, Deputy Director Chen of the shipyard led the Chinese and English guests on foot to the shipyard's dining hall for tea and refreshments. However, because the guests were quite crowded, additional seats were temporarily added. Champagne was shared in celebration.

(Director's Speech) During the seating, Deputy Director Chen gave a speech, saying: "Today, the British warship (Sandpiker Holk) is being launched. We are honored by the presence of all of you. This is the first time that our shipyard has built a British gunboat. We still hope to have this type of project again in the future. This ship was designed by the British Navy and built by the British Komin Factory. The factory has a close relationship with our shipyard, and many of its students have interned at our factory. This ship was supervised by (Holk Road) and (Hubg) of the Komin Factory, and they cooperated very well with our shipyard. We hope that this ship will exceed the original speed in the future. I would like to thank the Consul-General and all the officers of the British Navy, and I am especially grateful to Mrs. Mougen for naming and throwing the bottle. Please join me in a toast to wish you all a long life." After Chen's speech, the British naval officer and Mrs. Mougen gave speeches in response, and the guests dispersed, still taking the original steamer to disembark at the Customs Wharf.

(Overall Ship Structure) According to Mr. Weng Zuguang of the shipyard, the ship is 167 feet long, 30 feet wide, 5 feet deep, and has a draft of 2 feet. Its speed is 15 nautical miles per hour. The hull supervisor is Mr. (Nyhalt), and the machinery supervisor is Commander (Road). It is expected to be completed in one month after launching. After launching, it will immediately enter the dock for other construction work.

(Telegram to Beijing) After the ship was launched, Deputy Director Chen of the shipyard telegraphed Minister Chen Shaokuan in Nanjing, stating: "To Minister Chen Shaokuan of the Navy Department in Nanjing: Confidential. The British warship (Sandopiker) was successfully launched at 1:00 PM this afternoon (remainder omitted)."

Aircraft Engineer Wang Zhuchen Returns from Germany 140

Mr. Wang Zhuchen, the younger brother of Dr. Wang Yuanchen, the director of Jiangsu Provincial Hospital, graduated from the Mechanical Engineering Department of Tongji University. In 1928, he went to Germany at his own expense, first interning at a Berlin automobile factory, and then entered the Aircraft Engineering Department of Wanma Industrial University. He graduated in 1932 with a degree in aircraft and automobile engineering. After graduation, he interned at aircraft, automobile, and motor factories such as the Czech Wanertou, where he was proficient in the manufacture, repair, and driving of various aircraft.

Photo of Mr. Wang Guichen 141

Later, through the introduction of the factory, he was hired as an engineer at the Italian Caproni Aircraft Factory. All types of aircraft ordered by China from that country were personally tested by Mr. Wang. This time, Mr. Wang returned to China with his wife. Wanertou and other factories competed to hire him as the general manager in China, but Mr. Wang declined because he believed that selling foreign products would lead to the outflow of profits. Mr. Wang arrived in Shanghai on the Conte Rosso liner a few days ago and went to Beijing to visit his relatives and contact the central government about establishing his own aircraft manufacturing factory. He will go to Hangzhou in two weeks to test the No. 101 bomber newly purchased by the Aviation Administration from Italy.

Peng Boxun, director of the Ministry of Industry's National Goods Exhibition Hall, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday because the National Goods Exhibition will be held on the 20th of this month. Official business began yesterday, and the following measures were established: (1) The products of all manufacturers attending the exhibition will be exempt from taxes and transportation fees according to regulations, but they must be packed in boxes. (2) After the products of the exhibiting manufacturers are packed, they should be reported to the trade association or this office for registration, and this office will designate a transportation company to transport them to Nanjing. (3) The exhibition period will be one month. The exhibition space for each manufacturer will be provided by this association, and the fee per space will not exceed 30 yuan. (4) Each space will be provided with 20 light bulbs and two lamps by the association. If anyone wishes to install more, each lamp will be charged according to the price set by the electricity company.

Punishment for a Frivolous Youth 148

Lin Xuemei, a Ningbo woman in her early twenties, with a beautiful appearance, worked as a female worker at the Dongyouheng Cigarette Factory. Every day, she had to pass by Huichang on Tangshan Road. On the day before yesterday, the Huishan Police Department was informed and ordered detectives to arrest Li. Attorney Zhang Tianyin explained the case and presented the woman's damaged clothing as evidence, requesting investigation. Subsequently, the woman, Lin Xuemei, testified to the facts of the case. The defendant's confession was evasive. Judge Wu sentenced the defendant to eight months in prison as a warning.

Case of Apprentice's Tragic Death Transferred to Court 149

Judgment in the Case of Dai Jikui and His Concubine's Lawsuit 150

=Concubine's Request for Alimony Rejected=

=However, Management of Land and House Contract Valid=

Dai Jikui (also known as Dai Jigao), a resident of Nantong, is already in his fifties. Due to his years of business in Shanghai, his business has flourished, and he has accumulated some wealth. This has been coveted by his estranged concubine, Huang Cuixuan, leading to mutual lawsuits. According to the woman's complaint, in 1914, her former husband passed away. In 1917, she remarried Dai as his wife, and the following year, she gave birth to a daughter, Zhiying. However, after Dai took Hongying as a concubine in 1929, he suddenly turned against her. In the third month of 1929, they signed a separation agreement, stating that Dai would hand over 64.4 mu of sandy farmland in Changshu and a house in Sanxing Town, Washi, to her and her daughter to live in and manage. The rent from the land and house would be used for her annual living expenses. Later, because Dai did not repair the house, she could not live there and continued to reside in Shanghai with her daughter. In addition to paying for her daughter's tuition, Dai gave her 120 yuan per month for alimony. The rental income from the land and house, about 600 yuan per year, was also for her use. In recent years, due to famine, there was no rental income, and Dai stopped paying alimony. Therefore, she sued, requesting the court to order Dai Jikui to pay alimony at the rate of 120 yuan per month from January of this year until she reaches 65 years old in 1946, a one-time payment of 20,160 yuan. She also requested confirmation that the contract signed in March 1929 for the management of land and house is continuously valid. Dai Jikui hired lawyer Xuan Zhendong to argue that after Huang's husband died, he took pity on her poverty and lived with her. Since there was no matchmaker or any formal ceremony, she was not a formal spouse, and he was not legally obligated to provide alimony. He had been in the exchange business, which everyone knew. The woman's living situation should be assessed based on his economic affluence. In the past, when the business was profitable, he fulfilled all her requests. Even after the separation, her rent and daily expenses were still paid. Last year, the business failed, and he decided to move back to Nantong. However, the woman was extravagant and addicted to vices. Not only did she refuse to return with him, but on March 21st of this year, she gathered more than a dozen men and women to cause trouble. Afterwards, she falsely accused him of assault. Fortunately, the police station investigated and sternly reprimanded her. Later, while he was back in his hometown, she stole all his rosewood furniture and clothes and fled. As for the land and house in Changshu, when they separated, it was stated in the agreement that she would manage it on his behalf because he needed to do business in Shanghai. It was also noted that when he returned to his hometown, she should return the management rights. Since she has not returned to her hometown, how can she claim it as her own? He requested that the original lawsuit be rejected and filed a counterclaim against the woman, detailing the circumstances of entrusting Huang Cuixuan to manage the purchased land and house. He stated in the counterclaim that the original plaintiff is now returning to Tong with his entire family, and the management rights should be recovered. He requested that the contract be declared invalid. After repeated court sessions presided over by Judge Shen Hong of the First Special District Court, summoning both parties for interrogation, the judgment was announced yesterday afternoon. The plaintiff Dai Huang's request for the defendant to pay a one-time alimony of over 20,000 yuan was entirely rejected. However, the contract for the management of land and house was still considered valid. In addition, the defendant's counterclaim was also rejected.
