Case of Plotting to Assassinate Lytton

Three Principal Offenders Identified 151

丨The Assassination of Finance Minister Song Was Also Committed by These Three丨

More Than Twenty-Two People Have Been Detained

Sixteen of Them Were Released Yesterday Morning After Interrogation Proved Their Innocence

Two Were Transferred to the Second Special Court Due to the Case, and One Died of Illness

In October of last year, Chief Inspector You A'gen and Inspector Liu Junqing of the Old Zha Gate Police Station uncovered an organization plotting to assassinate a certain important person of the International Investigation Team. The location was at 90 Mintini Yin Road in the French Concession. They arrested on the spot: Long Lin (also known as Junwu, i.e., Shaoyuan), Ma Yijin (also known as Desheng), Tang Ming (also known as "Blind"), Ma Yinhe, Tian Zemin, Weng Xinwu, Chen Chunting, Li Yuncheng, Zhang Chun, Chen Jiesan, He Yinshan, Wan Jiayun, Liu Hanqing, Qin Tianyou, Xiang Ziyun, Xu Hongyuan, Wang Yunqiao, Su Zhian, Wang Bolin, Yu Minghai, Li Zhongfa, and Feng Guoqi, totaling twenty-two people. They confiscated one hand grenade, one pistol, and nine bullets. After detailed investigation, it was found that when Lord Lytton and his party of the League of Nations Investigation Team came to Shanghai and resided at the Cathay Hotel on Nanjing Road, these individuals, under the command of a certain military faction, also opened room 51 in the hotel, preparing several bombs, intending to throw them when Lord Lytton and the Chinese representative Dr. Gu Weijun went out. Fortunately, the Chinese military police and the concession authorities deployed tight security, preventing them from succeeding. Nevertheless, it was a close call. Furthermore, the case of the assassination attempt on Chinese Finance Minister Song Ziwen at the North Railway Station was also committed by Long Lin and others. They were handed over to the First Special District Court for adjudication and transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for interrogation. Those defendants found to be innocent would be sent back to facilitate investigation into any criminal behavior in the Public Concession. This has been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that after the interrogation of Long Lin and the other twenty-two people by the Local Court, it was determined that Long Lin, Tang Ming, and Wang Yunqiao were the principal offenders in the above two major cases. The others had no evidence of involvement in the crimes. Therefore, charges were filed against Long and the other three according to the law, and the rest were sent back to the Old Zha Gate Police Station. However, one of them, Chen Chunting, died of illness upon being sent back. Further investigation revealed that Ma Yijin and Li Zhongfa had committed multiple theft cases in the French Concession. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, where Judge Qian Hongye conducted the trial. Police lawyer Ru BaoYi explained the previous situation, stating briefly that Ma and Li were involved in theft cases in the French Concession. Today, the Second Special Court sent personnel to request their transfer. The police station did not object. The other sixteen people, including Ma Yinhe, Tian Zemin, and Weng Xinwu, were found to have no criminal behavior and should be released. Judge Qian then ordered that Ma Yijin and Li Zhongfa be handed over to the personnel sent by the Second Special Court for further investigation. The remaining sixteen people, including Ma Yinhe, were released together.

There is No Summer This Year

Yangtze River Water Level Reaches Thirty-Eight Feet 154

The Municipal Government Flood Relief Committee in Shanghai Has Received Reports

Whether a Disaster Will Occur Depends on the Weather in July

Since the major flood in Wuhan in 1931, continuous rain has fallen in Han Gao since the beginning of this month, causing the river water to rise sharply, reaching a level of thirty-eight feet. At the same time, according to reports from the observatory, there will be no extreme heat this summer. If the weather continues like this, the disasters of the past may inevitably be repeated today. Concerned about the social livelihood of the four provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi, the reporter yesterday specifically visited the National Government Flood Relief Committee on the Bund in Shanghai. According to its engineer, Lu Chao, April, May, and June are originally periods of heavy rainfall. The formation of the major flood in Wuhan in the past was due to heavy rainfall in May and June, followed by storms in July, making it difficult for the river to discharge and causing the river water to overflow, resulting in significant losses. Although they received a report on the 5th of this month stating that the river water had risen to a high of thirty-eight feet, it was not as high as the water level in previous years. Thirty-eight feet is only the same as in 1926. If the weather in July is good, without any wind or rain, the water will definitely recede at that time. Therefore, the water level, flow rate, and climate are all related. The waters of the Yangtze and Yellow Rivers are unlike other rivers; the water comes quickly and recedes quickly. According to their sources, it is all due to the melting snow on the mountains in Sichuan and Chongqing upstream after the rain in May and June, which flows downstream, making it difficult for the rivers to discharge for a time. Therefore, July is the discharge period. If the weather is sunny and mild in that month, there will definitely be no disaster. The height of the water level is unimportant due to the unique riverbed of the Yangtze River. The water levels near Xunhan often differ by as much as four feet. Even in Chongqing, the water level is more than five hundred feet higher than that of Wusong at the downstream end. Yichang and Wusong also differ by about two hundred feet. As for the embankments built by this committee, since the major flood in 1931, the damage along the river has been quite significant. After active repairs by this committee, the embankments in Wuhu, Wuhan, and Jiujiang, etc., will all be completed by the end of this month. The built embankments are all higher and thicker than before, by three to four feet. Therefore, even if the water is as high as in previous years, it will definitely be difficult to overflow the embankments. The lock works are more complicated and will not be completed until the end of September. Therefore, the current state of the river water depends on the weather in July. This committee has branches in Wuhan, including the Jianghan Bureau and the Jianggan Bureau. They have been instructed to pay attention at all times and report accordingly.

The Alarming Physical Defects of Students in This City 157

丨Statistics from the Health Bureau's Inspection丨

The Municipal Health Bureau, for the purpose of maintaining the health of students, is currently jointly working with the Education Bureau to handle school health and health education work. At yesterday's municipal meeting, Health Bureau Director Li reported that, up to recently, a total of 31,050 students had been examined. Those suffering from trachoma accounted for more than 60%, those suffering from dental diseases accounted for more than 53%, those with poor eyesight accounted for more than 22%, those with poor hearing accounted for more than 6%, those suffering from skin diseases accounted for more than 3%, those with lung diseases accounted for more than 2%, and those with heart diseases accounted for more than 1%. Only 14% of the students are physically healthy, meaning that on average, 86 out of every 100 people suffer from illness or have defects. This shows the fragility of our country's citizens' physique, and it is urgently necessary to remedy it. Although measures have been taken to treat them, the effects are difficult to achieve due to limited funding and personnel. It is also heard that the Health and Education Bureaus are actively discussing measures to facilitate the treatment of students and maintain the health of young people, so as not to hinder their ability to study and improve their efficiency in serving the country in the future.

Fierce Battle Against Thieves on Columbia Road 158

Resulted in the Capture of Two Thieves

A local woman, Qian Jinshi, is 55 years old. Her husband died early. She lives at 1 Hu Jiazhai, Hongqiao Road, West Shanghai. She has a daughter who has been betrothed and is about to marry. Therefore, Qian specifically prepared a dowry and jewelry for her daughter, which was extremely rich. However, the area is close to the wilderness. A group of neighbors, seeing such a rich dowry, could not help but admire it. The news quickly spread throughout the village and was heard by bandits. Suddenly, at about 7 AM yesterday, while the family had not yet gotten up, three bandits went to rob them. Two bandits were armed with pistols, and one unarmed person stood guard outside the door. They all spoke with a Jiangbei accent. After entering the door, they rushed into Qian's bedroom, forbidding her from making any noise, and searched everywhere. They left after about half an hour. Seeing that there was another room next to Qian's bedroom, they turned back into the room of Xu Shenshi, who lived with Qian, and plundered it before leaving. When the victims saw the bandits leaving, they quickly reported to the nearby Sixth District, Second Branch. The director of the branch urgently dispatched a senior police officer to pursue them. However, when the bandits were escaping, they saw a villager carrying a shoulder pole coming towards them. They drew their guns and ordered the villager to stop. They stole three silver dollars from him and fled. The villager urgently followed them, and when he chased them to the intersection of Columbia Road and Anheshi Road in the Public Concession, Police Officer 353 of the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station and Police Officer 1000, both Chinese and Western, happened to be patrolling in a vehicle. Seeing the villager's frightened expression, the Western police officer stopped the car and asked what was going on. The villager reported the robbery. Therefore, the Western police officer blew his whistle madly, notifying the nearby police officers. Then they drove back along the original road to pursue them. They saw a person running frantically ahead. The Western police officer ordered him to stop. Unexpectedly, the person was a bandit. Seeing that there were police officers behind him, he panicked and took out a pistol from his arms, opening fire on the Western police officer and others. The Western police officer and others also returned fire. After a fierce battle, the bandit saw that his ammunition was running out and, fearing arrest, hastily threw the stolen goods and pistol into the rice field beside the road to escape. However, he was still caught up and arrested by the Western police officer. He picked up the stolen goods and a pistol and took them to the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station. Under interrogation by the police chief, he confessed that his name was Wu Renru, 24 years old, from Anhui. He used to work as a tea server on the Dehe Wheel, but he had recently lost his job. He admitted to robbing the Qian family and others without hesitation. He also revealed the names of two accomplices, Zhu Chunhai, from Anhui, who lived at 3 Qian De Lane, Changping Road, and a man surnamed Chen, who lived at Yinghua Lane, Robert Road. After obtaining the confession, the police immediately dispatched police officers to arrest them. They arrested Zhu Chunhai, but the bandit surnamed Chen had already fled after receiving the news. At the same time, the Sixth District Police Station also received the news. Because the incident occurred within the jurisdiction of the district, they immediately reported it to the Public Security Bureau and sent personnel to the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station to welcome the captives. After an interrogation, they sent personnel to escort them to the General Bureau for further investigation.

Temporary Postponement of Park Price Increase by the Public Works Bureau 159

丨Female Employees Not Hired in Children's Parks for Now丨

The Public Works Committee of the Public Works Bureau discussed the issue of park ticket prices for next year at its last meeting. In 1931, 67,696 long-term tickets were sold, and in 1932, 51,039 were sold. The value of the long-term tickets and the retail tickets at the entrance is quite different, so some people advocated increasing the long-term tickets to two yuan. According to the report of the Director of the Public Works Department, the Zhaofeng Park has the most visitors on Sundays and public holidays. During the Dragon Boat Festival on May 28th, it reached more than 30,000 people, but it is not crowded on weekdays. After studying the matter, the committee members did not consider an increase necessary and decided to postpone the matter until the end of this year for further discussion. This decision has been adopted by the board of directors. Furthermore, the Women's Federation suggested that two Western women be hired in the Zhoushan Park on a trial basis to monitor children and maintain order. According to the Director of the Public Works Department, if this is implemented, it must also be done in at least two other children's parks. Such services are common in other large cities, but in this city, there are concerns that communication difficulties may arise due to language barriers. The need is not urgent at this time, so it seems appropriate to postpone it. After discussion by the committee, it was decided that the park management personnel do not need to be changed. This proposal has also been approved by the board of directors on the 7th.

Zhao Ruquan Case Opens

Celebrated Actors Gather in Court 160

Jia Biyun and Zhao Junyu Both Testified in Court

Huang Huiting and Xu Junfu Are Suspected of Embezzlement

Zhao Ruquan, a stage actor at the Samsung Theater, was originally the backstage manager of the theater and also managed the finances. The front desk accountant paid all the surplus from the daily income, after expenses, to Zhao Ruquan for safekeeping. In addition, the advertising fees for advertisements printed on the curtains of the theater were mostly collected by Zhao and not recorded in the accounts by the accountant. Recently, Zhou Bingchen, the manager of the theater, checked the accounts and found that Zhao was suspected of various acts of fraud. The concrete evidence included the aforementioned advertising fees, totaling more than 1,200 yuan. He hired lawyers Chen Tingrui and Du Jimei to file an embezzlement charge against Zhao. After investigation by the police, he applied to the First Special District Court for an arrest warrant. One night, in the middle of the night, he specially sent Chinese and Western detectives to the theater. At the time, Zhao was playing Ouyang De in the Peng Gong An play and was arrested while performing on stage. He was sent to court the next day and detained. Until the previous Saturday, Zhao hired lawyers Jiang Yiping and Liu Shichao to appear in court and post bail, which was approved. He was released on bail pending trial. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Feng Shide held the third hearing. Police lawyers Bo Liang and Ru BaoYi, representing the prosecution, and the lawyers Chen, Du, Jiang, and Liu, representing Zhou and Zhao, respectively, appeared in court. In addition, other shareholders of the theater hired lawyer Wu Linkun to attend the hearing. The friends and relatives of both sides who went to listen were still very crowded. Celebrated actors Jia Biyun and Zhao Junyu, being shareholders of the theater and having worked with Zhao Ruquan, were summoned to testify. Judge Feng first questioned the witness Mao Haishan about Zhao Ruquan's income from advertising fees without recording them in the accounts. Mao's answers were vague. He then summoned Zhao Junyu, who gave a detailed account of the functions of the accountant and the defendant in the theater. Regarding the advertising fees, he said that the defendant had reported them at two meetings, one on December 29th of last year and the other in early April of this year, and had presented the savings passbook from the Siming Bank to his colleagues. However, Zhou Bingchen did not attend the meetings. Jia Biyun was also questioned, and her statement did not differ much from Junyu's. According to the defendant Zhao Ruquan's testimony, they were too busy with the performances to hold any meetings. They were just casual gatherings. Regarding the advertising fees, he had reported them to the shareholders and had a savings passbook to prove it. How could Zhou Bingchen not know? He informed the accountant of everything that happened in the accounting office every day, and he had also notified him of the meetings, but he did not attend. As for the interest on the guarantee deposit from the power company, the accounting office entrusted me to collect it. It totaled only more than 370 yuan, and I immediately informed the accountant to register it after receiving it, etc. The court then summoned Huang Huiting and Xu Junfu, the two accountants, and questioned them briefly. Police lawyer Ru BaoYi then said that Huang and Xu were also suspected of embezzlement. Before filing charges, he requested that they be ordered to post bail to prevent them from escaping. Lawyer Jiang Yiping then stated that the accountant Zhao currently auditing the accounts was hired by the plaintiff. For the benefit of the defendant, he requested that the defendant also be allowed to hire an accountant to conduct a joint review to ensure fairness. Judge Feng then ordered the police that if they had any questions for Huang and Xu, they were allowed to summon them at any time and arrest them immediately if they disobeyed. Before filing charges, they were temporarily exempted from posting bail. The case was adjourned and will be heard again after the audit report is completed.

Follow-up on Police Shooting and Killing 162

Compensatory Settlement with the Deceased's Family

Di Chuanxiao, a fourth-class police officer numbered 2350 of the Fourth District General Bureau of Zhabei, was assigned to patrol at the fifth guard post on Datong Road at 3 PM on the 5th of this month. While standing in front of the Zhengchang Rice Shop, he accidentally touched the trigger while wiping his gun, and the bullet hit Zhou Zhangwen, the shop's clerk, as reported in this newspaper on the 6th of this month. Subsequently, the police district believed that the police officer had injured someone and needed to provide compensation. They summoned Zhou Zhouwen, the younger brother of Zhou Zhangwen, to the bureau. After negotiations, the police agreed to pay 100 silver dollars as compensation, and persuaded the shop owner to give 250 silver dollars, but wanted the shop owner to pay the 100 dollars first. The shop owner declined, stating that giving 250 dollars for no reason, as well as coffin and funeral expenses, was already a significant amount, and politely declined the 100 dollars offered by the police, requesting that they find another way to raise it. Well-wishers were very displeased and taught the deceased's brother to claim that the police officer played with the gun because of the shop owner's encouragement, in order to implicate them. The district chief believed that the police officer was not a child, and how could he handle a gun based on other people's teasing? On the one hand, he reached a settlement with the deceased's family regarding the compensation, and on the other hand, he presented the police officer to the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday,

he was transferred to the Local Court for interrogation.

Red Cross Relief for North China Refugees 163

The Shanghai branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society received a telegram yesterday from the Tianjin branch of the society, stating that since the signing of the truce agreement, although the fighting in the front lines has stopped, the number of refugees within the customs is increasing daily. The number of elderly and young people crowding into Tianjin has reached more than 30,000 and they urgently need financial assistance for relief. After receiving the telegram, the General Association immediately replied, agreeing to find ways to allocate 400 large bags of relief rice and 100 boxes of relief clothing to be used for relief of the refugees. It is planned to ship them to Tianjin soon. It is reported that since the outbreak of war in North China, the association has allocated a total of 5,000 yuan to the Tianjin branch for the treatment of wounded soldiers and the relief of refugees. The Tianjin branch has also sent detailed reports to the General Association by telegram.

Lawyer Chao Kun Covered in Dung 166

丨It's Not Easy Being a Lawyer in Shanghai丨

Yang Yinghou, residing in Yang Yinghou's residence at Jingxiu Road, within the Old West Gate, formerly arranged for Tao Fengdi (currently 22 years old) to leave her registered household and become his wife. This arrangement lasted for five years, but their love eventually soured. Tao Fengdi then engaged lawyer He Sui to file a lawsuit in the criminal division of the District Court, alleging restriction of freedom. She claimed that after becoming intimate with Yang, she had been subjected to abuse and imprisoned in a wooden cage. Prior to the hearing, Yang Yinghou commissioned lawyer Zhu Fang to publish a notice, claiming that Tao had absconded with over a hundred yuan worth of clothing and accessories on the 27th of last month. Therefore, the plaintiff considered it defamation and changed the request to one of defamation of character. Judge Yang Qianchang held a court session, and the defendant engaged lawyer Chao Kun to appear in court for defense. The judge advised them to settle out of court, but the defendant did not proceed. Therefore, the court debate continued yesterday afternoon. At 2:00 PM, Tao Fengdi and lawyer He arrived at the court to await the hearing, while the defendant Yang Yinghou and lawyer Chao Kun arrived late at 3:30 PM in Chao's car. As soon as the car door opened and Chao Kun stepped out on the roadside, a man dressed in short blue cloth shirt and pants suddenly approached. He held a round lead bucket about two feet high with a lid (similar to a rice bucket). He removed the lid and placed the bucket over Chao Kun's head. The man then fled swiftly, disappearing without a trace. Unexpectedly, the bucket contained a load of rotten dung, and it was stale. Lawyer Chao was as if receiving a "baptism of mud," with thick dung covering his head, body, and feet. Fortunately, he was wearing a straw hat, so his hair and face remained relatively clean. He immediately discarded his hat, removed his long gown, and was left with only a small short shirt. His pants, feet, and briefcase were still covered in yellow stains. He rushed to the courthouse bathroom to wash himself clean, but a lingering odor remained. The hearing for Yang Yinghou's case had already begun in the first courtroom. Lawyer Chao immediately recounted what had happened, stating that today's events were too coincidental, suggesting suspicion toward the plaintiff's side. Lawyer He Sui responded that the plaintiff had been in the courthouse earlier and was a woman, so Lawyer Chao's attack was by a man, and could not be guessed at. Thereupon the judge ordered Lawyer Chao to present the main text of the case, immediately declaring that if Tao Fengdi withdrew the lawsuit, they could discuss a resolution. However, Tao Fengdi refused to withdraw. The official then persuaded them that both parties were willing to terminate their relationship, and since it was not a formal union, it could not be considered formal. The judge suggested that Yang Yinghou provide Tao Fengdi with 200 yuan to fully resolve the five-year de facto marriage. However, Tao Fengdi refused. The debate then concluded, and the official announced that a settlement was still being pursued before the verdict. Both parties agreed and left the court. It was said that the person who dumped the dung had been sitting on the road for four hours, and there was also a basket disguised as a vendor selling zongzi, intending to cause trouble.

Letter to the Editor 174

To the Editor: I have read the news in the "Collection of Fishery Dues for Construction Costs to be Mediated Today" section of your local news column on June 7th, which is far from the truth. I fear that outsiders will misunderstand and cause confusion. I hereby report the facts. Since the establishment of the Collection Office for Fishery Construction Costs of the Fisheries Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industrial Affairs, Jiangsu and Zhejiang Districts, it has been announced that the principle of "taking from fishing and using for fishing" has been established, and the method of collection has been determined, assigning the fish market to collect dues on behalf of the government based on price. Our colleagues believe that this was reviewed and approved by the Central Political Conference, and the original principle was "taking from fishing and using for fishing." As the name implies, "taking from fishing" should naturally be paid by fishermen in the fishing area. Our colleagues are not collection agencies, so how can we collect dues on behalf of the government based on price and bear obligations that we should not bear? At the same time, fish merchants from various ports have protested, sending letters and telegrams, unanimously denying collection by the market. However, the collection office has refused to comply with the Ministry's orders and has forcibly detained goods. Although the goods were returned after arguing with reason, the fresh goods were delayed, resulting in significant losses. Later, Mr. Du Yuesheng, Mr. Yu Zuoting, and Mr. Yu Qiaqing strongly advocated for fairness and took the initiative to mediate. However, the officials insisted on their preconceived notions, resulting in unsuccessful negotiations. This is the general situation of the process. Your newspaper said, "Now, four fish markets, including Dacheng Yuanchang, have colluded with stone urn fish merchants in Shipu to unreasonably oppose, clearly being manipulated by a certain country, sowing discord, and there are treacherous merchants acting as accomplices, secretly organizing institutions and attempting to manipulate things behind the scenes," etc. Such absurd remarks are not based on any evidence. However, the facts are all there, and those who are knowledgeable will laugh at them. We have always admired your newspaper for leading the masses and upholding justice. Please publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section to correct public opinion and report the facts. Sincerely, The Sixteen Fish Markets, including Dacheng Fish Market, etc. June 9, 22.

Special Announcement

"Summary of Japan's Wartime Economy" from the Shen Bao Series 176

Compiled and translated by Luo Shu

208 pages, six-point paper size, actual price 60 cents

This book is compiled and translated by Mr. Luo Shuhe based on the "Complete Picture of Japan's Wartime Economy" compiled by Japan's Toyo Keizai Shinpo, with reference to other important materials. The content is extremely rich and valuable, especially in the current extremely tense Sino-Japanese relations. On the one hand, we must have a precise review of the Japanese lineup, and on the other hand, we must have a comparative assessment of our own strength. At the same time, we should have a clear observation of the position of Japan's capabilities in the entire world view. To complete these tasks, this book can just give us considerable help. The main content of this book is introduced below: The book is divided into five chapters. Chapter 1 "War and National Mobilization Plan". Divided into four sections, the first section explains the significance of national general mobilization. Modern warfare, due to special technological advancements in the industry, has invented many new weapons, which have changed the method of combat, and the scope of war has expanded to dozens or even hundreds of times more than before. The so-called national general mobilization plan is following the expansion of this scope of war. Section 2 describes the method of national general mobilization. It first describes the types of national general mobilization, including talents, money, and military supplies. In the war, a large number are needed and must be concentrated in a very short period of time; The second section describes the experience of the belligerent countries in the European War in national general mobilization, and divides it into national mobilization, industrial mobilization, and transportation mobilization. In this table, we can see how much the government's control ability can be expanded in wartime. The third section explains the relationship between capitalism and national general mobilization, and clearly points out that there is an inseparable close connection between war and capitalism. The fourth section describes the Japanese Military Industry Mobilization Law. The Japanese Military Industry Mobilization Law is an extremely important document in Japan. This chapter records the entire content and adds a brief explanation. From here, we can have a clear understanding of the basic form of Japan's military industry mobilization. Chapter 2 "The State of Japan's Military Industry". Provide a summary description of the entire state of Japan's military industry, divided into three sections: metal industry, machinery and equipment industry, and chemical industry. A detailed list of Japanese military factories is attached, which is very important for the investigation of Japan's national strength. Section 4 describes the various social consequences resulting from factory mobilization, pointing out that the surge in military supplies will inevitably cause confusion in production organization, high prices, increased exploitation of labor, and increased burden on the people, explaining that war is enough to "promote the maturity of political crisis," clearly telling us the weaknesses of capitalism. Chapter 3 is "An Anatomy of Japanese Government-Operated Enterprises". This chapter is connected to the description of the state of Japan's military industry in the previous chapter, and provides a detailed review of Japanese military enterprises directly under the government's jurisdiction, that is, for "Japanese government-run enterprises, especially in the field of enterprises, on what social and economic basis they originated, what their historical development process is, what their content is, and what is their current task?" to conduct an investigation. A total of six sections are described. The first section explains the definition and types of government-run enterprises, which is the outline of this chapter. The second section describes the occurrence of Japanese government-run enterprises, giving a historical outlook on the process of the occurrence of Japanese government-run enterprises, and at the same time it tells us how huge the content of Japanese government-run enterprises is. The third section describes the content of Japanese government-run enterprises, divided into the investment of government-run enterprises, government-run factories and laborers, the names of Japanese government-run factories, their locations, main products, and the distinction and number of male and female employees, and government-run mines. From here, we can see Japan. Section 4 describes the relationship between Japanese government-run enterprises and national finances, pointing out that Japanese government-run enterprises are based on strong finances, that is, the importance of the national economy, and at the same time, we can see how important non-productive military industry occupies in the entire industry. Section 5 mainly describes the status of government-run enterprises. Japanese major government-run enterprises; communications, national railways, ironworks, monopoly, naval and army factories, land, etc., are explained in sections on the historical development process and the overview of their content. The breadth of the content and the strength of the economic power of Japan's major government-run enterprises can be seen from this. Section 6 explains the relationship between government-run enterprises and national control, pointing out that the "operational trend of Japanese government-run enterprises originated in the Meiji Restoration era, not only in industry, but also in more important military reasons, and adopted an extreme protection policy", "This is why the wartime economy is valued", "The so-called control is the monopoly of state capital" and its purpose is to "develop the military industry." Once a war occurs, "both public and private economies are placed under the new wartime establishment, especially the government-run enterprises that are easier to reorganize are more fully promoted in this direction." This is the content of Japan's wartime economy. Chapter 4 "The Structure of Wartime Economy", points out that Japan's budget has reached the stage of "wartime economy" due to its continuous invasion of our country, and is described in eight sections. The first section explains the situation of the sudden increase in Japan's budget in 1931 due to the Shenyang Incident; The second section describes the large expansion of Japan's implementation budget in 1932, "The implementation budget in 1932 has a very strong color of wartime finance"; The third section continues to explain that the increase in this budget in Japan is due to the expansion of military expenditures. At present, Japan has almost "devoted all its efforts to military preparations" and "temporarily delayed everything". On the one hand, the economic panic is becoming more and more profound, the income is decreasing, the military expenditure is increasing, and the budget is becoming more and more insufficient. Therefore, the Japanese government has added an emergency budget, but this increase in budget is still actually used for military purposes. Sections 4, 5 and 6 detail the budget status in Japan and the issuance of public bonds due to insufficient budget. Section 7 describes Japan's wartime budget in 1933. From here, we can see some shocking figures. The editor said: "With such a large expenditure on time, according to Japan's national strength and the general situation at the moment, it cannot be said to be a miracle!" Indeed, this is a miracle! Chapter 5 "The Trend of Wartime Monetary Policy". Describes Japan's preparation for various policies on inflation caused by the war, such as the "Amendment Law in the Bank of Japan Exchange Voucher Regulations", such as the "Bank of Japan "Payment Money" Bill", such as the "Law on the Calculation of Government Bond Prices," such as the "Law on Preventing Capital Flight", etc. This chapter records their full text and adds detailed explanations. To show that Japan is now completely prepared for war, and its economic state bears the nature of a wartime economy. A table of Japan's main resource supply and demand statistics is attached at the end, which is of great reference value. The above is a glimpse of the main content of the book. Of course, this is just a brief description, and it cannot be said that it is the essence of the whole book. In short, this book is worth reading, whether it is for specialized research or for the supply of general youth knowledge, this book can fulfill its due responsibility, especially at present, this book is definitely not a common reading material, this can be asserted. According to Mr. Luo himself in the afterword, "From the good intentions, Japan has been our neighbor for thousands of years, and the relationship in the most recent 50 or 60 years is particularly close. We should pay more attention to and study its actual situation, especially Japan expressed in numbers. From the non-good intentions, Japan has put us on the operating table and repeatedly dissected and analyzed us countless times. Although its understanding of China is only flat and superficial, it has grasped the key points, at least it can grasp the reality; however, our understanding of Japan is not very much, although we regard it as a hypothetical enemy 丨丨It has become a frontal enemy in the past year and a half, and is in opposition in economic, political, and military terms. There is no hope of reconciliation in the near future, but our understanding of it is not very much. We should examine Japan's wartime preparations more. The motivation for compiling this booklet is also here." It can be seen from this that the value of this book is one aspect. There are more than fifty tables in the statistics.

Middle School Graduation Exams in Beijing are Inevitable 177

Report by the Social Affairs Bureau to the Principals of Each Middle School

(Nanjing, 9th) The Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau convened the principals of public and private middle schools at 9 p.m. to report that the bureau intends to hold a graduation exam for each high school, and that high school students who do not wish to attend the graduation exam will give up their qualifications for graduation. The exam location was originally divided into four locations, but for convenience, more locations will be divided in the future to avoid disturbances from a small number of malicious individuals. In the event that there are still disturbances after the multi-division area, the military and police will severely suppress them. Please advise the students to go to the exam on time, and it was decided that on the morning of the 10th, the principals of each school would lead one or two high school student representatives to the bureau, and the bureau chief would admonish them. According to the talks of the school leaders, the Provincial Beijing High School and Beijing Women's High School are scheduled to hold the graduation exam by the Jiangsu Education Department from the 11th, which is no longer a problem. In addition, there is no problem with the junior high school graduation exam in various schools in Beijing. That is, the situation in each high school is different, and only a few students do not want to participate in the graduation exam. Now each school is holding an internal graduation exam. At first, some high school students in each school went on strike, but after persuasion, there was no foundation, and it was decided to hold the exam as usual on the 12th. It is reported that the high school student representatives of each school still held a meeting at Zhongying Middle School on the afternoon of the 9th.

Ministry of Education Orders Rectification of Peking University, Afterwards 178

Acting President Xu Songming Formally Resigns

Various Colleges Discuss Various Steps

Yan Zikai Seeks Instructions on Handling the Aftermath

(Special Dispatch from Peiping) Peking University recently received instructions from the Ministry of Education to rigorously rectify all colleges under its jurisdiction. Except for the Colleges of Agriculture, Engineering, and Medicine, which will continue to operate as usual and enroll students as usual, many other changes will be made. The College of Arts and Sciences for Women, due to the small number of students in each class and the uneconomical use of funding and teachers, is ordered to make efforts to reduce and merge departments and report to the Ministry for approval. The Russian Law and Russian Economic departments of the College of Law will be abolished, and enrolled students will be merged into other departments. Enrollment in the Political Science department will be suspended. The College of Commerce will suspend enrollment this year and temporarily maintain the status quo. The College of Art will be closed immediately. The affiliated high school, as there are many such schools in Peiping, will also be closed. Students of the school will be given certificates to facilitate their transfer to other schools. After receiving these instructions, the Peking University Office immediately distributed them to the various colleges and the high school, ordering them to comply and handle the matter. It also telegraphed Principal Xu Songming, who was in Beijing, seeking instructions on everything. Details of each item are recorded separately as follows:

Instructions from the Ministry of Education 179

It is noted that this university, in addition to the Colleges of Agriculture, Engineering, and Medicine, should suspend enrollment in other colleges in order to rectify them. This was previously ordered in the Ministry's Instruction No. 5728 of the previous year, which was to be followed. Now, according to the university's report on the general situation for the 20th year, the College of Arts and Sciences for Women has both arts and science departments, with divisions for mathematics, physics, chemistry, Chinese, English, philosophy, economics, history, and music, totaling thirty-one classes with a total of three hundred and twelve students in the entire college, averaging only ten students per class. The funding and teachers are not economical, so each department should make efforts to reduce and merge departments, and report to the Ministry for approval. The College of Law originally had departments of Law, Political Science, and Economics, as well as Russian Law and Russian Economics. Now, with the rectification of the judiciary and economic construction underway, the Law and Economics departments are still needed, but the Russian Law and Russian Economics departments should be abolished, and enrolled students should be merged into other departments. Enrollment in the Political Science department should still be suspended, so that all efforts can be focused on enriching the Law and Economics departments. The College of Commerce was originally established to cultivate talents for frontier trade. However, there are currently quite a few such talents, so enrollment should be temporarily suspended this year. The College of Art was ordered to be closed earlier and should be closed immediately this year. There are many affiliated high schools in Peiping, so there is no need to continue operating them. The students of the affiliated high school should be given certificates of completion to facilitate their transfer to other schools, so that the school can be closed. This order is hereby issued and the university is instructed to comply with it and report back for record.

Chen Zhongping Discusses Measures 180

This reporter met with Chen Zhongping, secretary of Peking University, to discuss the Ministry of Education's instructions to rectify Peking University. The instructions were issued on the 2nd and arrived at the school on the 5th. On the 6th, the instructions were forwarded to each college. The Ministry of Education's plan to rectify Peking University was decided last year, but due to various difficulties, it could not be fully implemented. With the summer vacation approaching this year, how to handle the matter in the future is naturally a problem. Principal Xu Songming's trip to Beijing was to meet with the Minister of Education to discuss this issue. However, the ministry's order was issued while the principal was en route to Beijing. Currently, the university office is forwarding the ministry's order to each college and the affiliated high school. Each college will discuss the rectification measures in detail. At the same time, they will telegraph Principal Xu, who is in Beijing, to seek instructions on how to handle the matter. It is hoped that Principal Xu will be able to discuss the matter in detail with the Ministry of Education in Beijing and obtain appropriate measures. Once Principal Xu returns to the school, he will convene a joint meeting of the deans of each college to discuss the matter thoroughly, it is said.

Xu Songming Has Resigned 181

After arriving in Beijing, Xu Songming, the acting president of Peking University, learned that the Ministry of Education had issued instructions to Peiping, stating that the Colleges of Agriculture, Engineering, and Medicine should continue to enroll students as usual, while the College of Arts and Sciences for Women should reduce and merge departments, the College of Law should abolish two departments, the College of Commerce should temporarily suspend enrollment this year, and the College of Art and the affiliated high school should both be closed. Xu then decided to resign and telegraphed this intention to Peiping. On the 8th, the University President's Office notified each college and the affiliated high school with the following original text: "Respectfully, we have just received a telegram from Principal Xu, briefly stating that he arrived in Beijing this morning and learned that the Ministry of Education had issued an order for winter reform. He immediately submitted a request to the Ministry to resign and asked to convey this to each dean, Songming. Accordingly, we are writing to you for your information. In addition to distributing this to other parties, this is addressed to the deans of each college and the affiliated high school, Peking University President's Office."

Art College Convenes Meeting to Discuss 182

The issue of closing the College of Art had been brewing for two years. The former dean, Yang Zhongzi, professors, and student representatives had contacted the Ministry of Education separately, so it had not been resolved until this year. Now, the Ministry of Education has instructed Peking University that the College of Art had been ordered to be closed earlier and should be closed immediately this year. Upon hearing this news, the faculty, staff, and students of the College of Art gathered to discuss measures.

College Affairs Meeting: The College of Art held a college affairs meeting at noon on the 8th. Committee members Yan Zikai, Luo Jiongzhi, Peng Peimin, Ding Naigang, Zhou Zhaoxiang, Tian Lin, Yang Zhongzi, and Gao Leyi were present. Yan Zikai chaired the meeting, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) To request Dean Yan to go to Beijing to contact the Ministry of Education regarding college affairs. Resolved and passed. (2) To send a telegram to the Ministry of Education requesting the maintenance of art education. Resolved and passed. (3) To elect professors as representatives to petition the government in the near future. Resolved to discuss this at the next meeting. The meeting adjourned at 3 PM.

Telegram to the Ministry of Education: To Minister Wang of the Ministry of Education in Nanjing, and Principal Xu of Peking University: We have just received the ministry's order stating that the College of Art had been ordered to be closed earlier and should be closed immediately this year. Upon investigation, this college has never received an order to close. Previously, due to the change to a specialized school, this college experienced difficulties, and representatives were sent to the ministry to explain the situation. As a result, the college system was maintained, and the existing classes were allowed to graduate before the change to a specialized school was made. Therefore, there was an order for gradual closure, which is not related to closure. Peiping is a cultural area, and there are no other national art schools in the surrounding provinces. Since there is no redundancy, why is it being cancelled? If it is said that the college is not being managed well, this is due to various political influences. Moreover, in recent years, the college has been reorganized and seems to be no worse than other colleges. By what standards is it being ordered to close? There are currently more than two hundred students in the second and third grades of each department. Closing the college midway would leave them with no place to transfer and would render them abandoned. The previous order to stop recruiting new students has already threatened the interruption of art education. If the college is closed further, it would be tantamount to crippling it. In accordance with the principle of equal national education, this should not be the case. We fear that the minister is newly appointed and has not examined the original details, leading to this order. Therefore, we are providing a detailed explanation and respectfully request that you reconsider and handle this matter impartially, so that we can be reassured. The remainder will be presented in person by Dean Yan and the elected representatives in a joint statement. Signed by all members of the College Affairs Meeting of the College of Art of Peking University. Yan Zikai Speaks: This reporter visited Yan Zikai, Dean of the College of Art, to inquire about the Ministry's measures. The response was as follows: The college affairs meeting today resolved to request me to go to Beijing. Although I suffer from rheumatism, I will have to go to Beijing despite my illness. I will be leaving for the south tomorrow or the day after. The Ministry of Education's order stated that the College of Art should be closed immediately, but there were no further details. I will go to Beijing to visit Minister Wang and seek instructions on how to handle the matter. As a student of art, I certainly cannot sit idly by and watch art education be interrupted. Moreover, after our college was reorganized, everything was on track. I don't know why it is now being ordered to close. Closing the college is one problem, and how to handle the students after the closure is another problem. Whether there is a possibility of continuing to operate the art school is also a question for the Ministry. I will discuss this matter thoroughly with Minister Wang. First, I hope that the College of Art will not be closed. Second, I will seek instructions on handling the aftermath, it is said.

The intention is to temporarily suspend enrollment, not to close the college. The issue of suspending enrollment is first, a problem for the entire Peking University, and second, it requires consideration by the faculty and staff of the College of Commerce. Our college was established only a year ago after the change to commerce, and we are in the process of cultivating talents for frontier trade. As for the number of talents, it is still unknown as it is far from the graduation period. The Ministry of Education's order to temporarily suspend enrollment this year may be due to the financial difficulties of the College of Commerce, but how to proceed will be discussed in detail by the college affairs meeting, it is said.

Gu Deng of the Women's College Speaks 184

According to Gu Cheng, Dean of the College of Arts and Sciences for Women, the college's views on the Ministry's reduction and merger of departments are as follows: I had heard about the Ministry of Education's intention to reduce and merge the departments of our college when I was in Beijing before. This time, the Ministry's order to our college to make efforts to reduce and merge departments is probably based on the previous discussion, but it does not specify concrete measures. Which department should be reduced and merged will still be decided by our college based on the circumstances, and then reported to the Ministry for approval. College of Commerce Students Inspect German Mail Ship 194

The Shanghai College of Commerce has a batch of students attached to the Transportation Class, specializing in teaching the procedures of sea transport and the professional knowledge of commercial exchange and loading, which is essential for the development of domestic and foreign trade. The professors of the class believe that the transportation industry also emphasizes experience, which can make up for the inadequacy of knowledge. Therefore, it was decided to select outstanding students to conduct on-site inspections of foreign mail ships in Shanghai. It was decided that the Transportation Class of the college would contact the North German Mail Ship Company for observation matters.

The North German Lloyd Mail Ship Company, managed by the German merchant Meijing Times in this city, has a large presence in the Far East shipping industry, divided into cargo ships and mail ships. Among them, the 10,000-ton-class ships such as the Cebroqi and Difijielin are ships that emphasize both cargo and passengers. The transportation management and procedures on board are the most complete. The College of Commerce had previously obtained the company's consent and decided to send a class of students to the ship to inspect the cargo and passenger procedures of various transports today.

Yesterday, the North German Company's mail ship Cebroqi entered the port. It was the ship taken by Zhang Dianjiu, commander of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army, and others to return home. The passenger cabins and cargo holds of the ship are very new and are famous among the new foreign ships. The College of Commerce specially dispatched Professor Yang Dayi to lead 40 students from the Transportation Class to the Gaogong Hexiang Wharf this afternoon to conduct on-site inspections of the cargo and passenger procedures of the transport, in order to learn from each other. The Meijing Times Foreign Firm has assigned Chinese and German staff to the ship to guide, entertain, and explain, it is said.

Changes in Sports Weight Punching Match

Xue Molin Suddenly Suffers Setback 196

Defeated by Baja

Xie Gai Will Face Ganella

Punching matches are popular in Europe and the United States, and heavyweight matches are especially valued. In recent years, the authority on the world's heavyweight stage has always been the German Xue Molin and the American Xie Gai. After Jie Ke Tai Mushan fell behind, the heavyweight championship crown was always transferred to the heads of the two. Heroes create the times, and news has been spread remotely that the so-called German heavyweight punching master Xue Molin has suddenly been defeated by Mark Baja. Baja is an American from California, young and strong, and one of the contenders for this year's world heavyweight championship. On the 29th of this month, the Italian "giant" punching master Ganella will meet the American Xie Gai. The winner will compete with Baja, which is a scene of the world heavyweight championship.

The Grand Event of the Competition: Although the battle between Xue Molin and Baja is not a scene of the championship, it is extremely relevant to the future championship. Xue's defeat also means that he has lost his qualification for this year's championship. The two competed in New York on the 8th, with as many as 60,000 spectators. The ticket revenue was also as much as 250,000 yuan. The American economy is prosperous, although it has not yet recovered, but this grand event is enough to know how deep their preferences are. The competition was originally scheduled for fifteen rounds, but until the tenth round, after Xue Molin fell to the ground and got up again, the referee Molinawen stopped Xue Molin from competing again and judged the victory to Baja. At that time, Xue was really unable to deal with it after being knocked down and getting up again. If he had forced it, it would have been in vain.

Process of Failure: In the first and second rounds, the two were equally powerful. From the third round, Xue gradually showed signs of being invincible. In the fifth round, Xue gradually rose and took the lead. In the seventh round, Baja attacked fiercely again and gained the upper hand, and Xue showed weakness. In the eighth round, the situation reversed again, and Xue gained the upper hand. In the ninth round, Baja still cheered up, and Xue appeared clumsy in comparison. In the tenth round, Baja's powerful swing directly forced Xue to retreat to the side of the rope. With a punch with his right hand, Xue fell to the ground. The referee shouted the number. By the time he reached the ninth count, Xue got up, his knees were weak and powerless, and his breathing was short. He still wanted to fight again, but was stopped by the referee, and he was defeated. Baja weighed 203 pounds, and Xue weighed 189 and a quarter pounds. Baja's victory was partly due to this.

Donghua Football Team's Expedition to the Philippines (II) 200

Beating the Summer Champion Bohimi Two to Zero

A Water War After the Wind and Rain Shows Its Skills

Amazing Performances are Rarely Seen in the Philippine Stadium

(Our Correspondent in the Philippines, Wen Chu, From Manila)

The Donghua football team came to the Philippines. In the first game, it drew 2-2 with the Spanish Club. On June 1, in the second game, it defeated the Bandit Island Summer Champion Bohimi team by two to zero, which was very gratifying.

A Great Storm Forces Postponement 201

The second match, originally scheduled for May 30th, was set to see renewed conflict at the Carnival Grounds football field. However, the weather was uncooperative, with wind and rain throughout the morning and afternoon, turning the field into an impassable mire. This forced a postponement to the (1st) day. Many fans who had prepared to watch the Tung Wah athletes in their second match in Manila were disappointed and went home.

The Opponent's Strength Should Not Be Underestimated 202

The Bohemia Sports Association team are the champions of last year's Manila Summer Football Tournament's Whitebread Cup. The entire team has a fast-moving forward line and a solid defense. Recalling this year's selection of athletes to attend the Manila-Iloilo inter-city football competition, the team drew with Santa Mila in the preliminary round. Furthermore, six players from the Spanish club who played the first match against Tung Wah last Sunday came from this team. Each player is deeply familiar with Tung Wah's tactics and is determined to defeat Tung Wah.

Sunshine After the Storm 203

On the 1st, the weather was clear from morning to noon. At 2:30 PM, a sudden storm arrived, but by 5 PM, the sun was shining brightly and the weather was clear. Many fans assumed that the field would be flooded after the heavy rain and that the match would be postponed again. However, this was not the case. After the rain stopped, although the field was muddy, the organizers, seeing the clear sky and sunshine, believed a match was possible and ordered the game to proceed. They immediately summoned field staff, such as ticket sellers and gatekeepers, to their posts. Unfortunately, very few people knew about the match after the rain, so only a little over two hundred people bought tickets and entered the stadium. This was the lowest attendance record for an important football match in Manila's history. This can be attributed to the unpredictable weather.

Athletes Suffer on the Mire-Like Battlefield 204

Before 5 PM, the heavy rain continued to pour down. At 5 PM sharp, the sky finally cleared. The match, decided on short notice, was postponed and began at 5:30 PM. At that time, the sky was full of clouds, the entire field was muddy, and water accumulated in the low-lying areas. The ball was heavy, and the scene was extremely bleak.

Recollecting the Previous Match, Everyone is Cautious 205

The first match ended in a draw. Tung Wah was unfamiliar with the field. Due to weather conditions yesterday, each half was only thirty minutes long. Both sides chose their best players to compete. After sixty minutes of fierce fighting, from beginning to end, everyone was in a state of shock. The intensity of the performance was breathtaking, and the tension of the battle was exciting. Tung Wah, aware of the audience's disappointment from the first match, put on a performance that was like two different teams. Their forwards charged with vigor and vitality, and their defenders were as impenetrable as copper walls and iron barriers. It was truly admirable.

United as One, Collective Will Becomes a Fortress 206

Yesterday's opponent was determined to defeat Tung Wah. Therefore, at the beginning of the match, they applied intense pressure. After failing, they resorted to rough tactics to resist. In the second half, Tung Wah's goal was heavily harassed. Fortunately, goalkeeper Lu Zhong'en was calm and agile, and Feng Yunyou and Li Ning worked together to defend the flanks. In addition, Sun Sijing, Tu Kaiyuan, and Liang Shutang firmly defended the midfield, ensuring safety. As for the five forwards Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Hongguang, Li Yichen, made several amazing long shots, but unfortunately missed by a hair's breadth. Chen Yutian and Wan Xianghua had wonderful dribbling skills, especially Wan Xianghua's accurate corner kicks and crosses, which are rarely seen in the local football scene. In the second half, Chen Jiaqiu and Cao Qiuting interchanged dynamically, proving effective. Although Chen Yutian and Li Yichen scored the two goals for Tung Wah, without Wan Xianghua's passing, it is feared that they would not have succeeded. Therefore, when rewarding merit, Wan Xianghua's contribution should not be overlooked.

The Opponent's Ferocity is Alarming 207

The opponents chose experienced and skilled players. The left defender was the most outstanding, with strong legs and good dribbling skills. Tung Wah's first line of defense was often dribbled past, but Feng Yunyou's long kicks repeatedly repelled the attacks. The right center back relied on his tall physique to display his heading skills, but under Sun Sijing's surveillance, he could not show his skills. The other center forward, left winger, and left inside forward were all fast-running riders. However, they were too eager to score, so several good shooting opportunities were missed, which was useless. Their goalkeeper, Mr. Jia Xieya, was indeed agile. If it weren't for him, the opponent would have lost by at least six goals.

A Full-Scale Attack Begins at the Start of the Battle 208

At the sound of the whistle, the opponent took the offensive. The five forwards advanced in a series, but were intercepted by Sun Sijing halfway. He passed the ball far to Chen Yutian, who went solo towards the opponent's goal. The inside defender came out to resist and also passed the ball far to their left winger, whose shot was caught by Lu Zhong'en. The general audience thought that since the battle clouds had just opened and the situation was so intense, a major battle was in the offing.

Yutian Scores First with a Header, Breaking the Enemy's Goal 209

As the battle clouds opened, the opponent immediately launched an offensive, but our army swept them all out of bounds. At this time, our army displayed its long-range shooting skills. The ball hovered outside the opponent's goal. After four rounds of attacks, they resisted stubbornly, unable to score. The applause and cheers from the stands responded like echoes. Sure enough, Tung Wah got a corner kick opportunity. Wan Xianghua aimed and kicked accurately, landing right in front of the goal. Chen Yutian identified the target and rushed forward, heading the ball before it touched the ground. The ball flew into the net, and Jia Xieya, known as the Iron Gate of the Philippines, was at a loss. He seemed to think the ball came from the sky. Cheers and applause rose from all around, celebrating the victory. The goal was scored nearly twenty minutes into the game.

Taking Advantage of the Victory, Strive to be First 210

Having won a goal, Tung Wah's morale soared. The five forwards attacked more urgently, without the courteous and modest demeanor of the first match. They had already learned the lessons from the first match. In the previous match, they were too trusting, allowing the enemy to take advantage. They knew that they had to start with a fierce and strong strategy to succeed. Therefore, led by Li Yichen, the three armies directly attacked the enemy's fortress. Chen Hongguang, Li Yichen, and Chen Jiaqiu Wan Xianghua all gave excellent long-range shooting performances. For a time, the enemy's fortress was filled with the footprints of Tung Wah's athletes. Fortunately, Jia Xieya's rescue was effective. Although they did not lose another goal, the Spanish audience at the scene was quite shocked.

Continuing the Effort, Another Record is Set 211

After the break, the teams switched sides and continued the battle. Tung Wah replaced Chen Jiaqiu with Cao Qiuting. The opponent also replaced their left inside forward. Tung Wah still dominated. The five forwards probed left and right, seeking opportunities to attack. Li Yichen and Chen Hongguang advanced side by side. Li Yichen's long-range shooting and dribbling skills were reminiscent of Li Huitang. Once, he kicked from thirty yards away, hitting the corner of the goal and bouncing out. The enemy's Iron Gate was shocked. Later, Wan Xianghua, with Chen Yutian's assistance, charged forward from the left, as fast as lightning. The enemy's right defender could not catch up. He dribbled to a suitable spot and immediately crossed. Li Yichen went forward alone and kicked the ball in, falling to the ground. Even if the Iron Gate goalkeeper had the ability to turn the tide, he could not escape this kick.

The Battle Becomes Tighter at the Last Moment 212

The opponent was not a mediocre team. How could they be willing to be suppressed for long? A forward with the nickname "Long Legs Immortal" ordered the entire army to counterattack. His long passes were quite effective. The five forwards frequently besieged Tung Wah's goal. Lu Zhong'en in front of the goal suddenly saw the enemy's figure. He was overwhelmed with blocking the incoming balls, high and low. There were two close calls. Once, the enemy's center forward shot directly from fifteen yards in front of the goal. Lu Zhong'en reacted quickly and blocked the ball with his hand, sending it over the goal. Another time, the opponent launched a fast and low ball from the left. Lu Zhong'en could not reach it with his hand, so he kicked it out with his foot. After surviving these two dangerous moments, the entire team switched from attack to defense, becoming more cautious in order to stall for time. Therefore, the opponent's offense and defense were very fierce in the second half, but until the end of the game, they did not achieve any success.

Wireless Radio Weekly

Trying Out New Vacuum Tubes 217

— Ming Xiang

Are the vacuum tubes in your radio the latest model? If they are still the old type, then your radio has become outdated. Please replace them with the latest models as soon as possible, which will bring you unexpected results. The replacement method is written below:

227丨丨 This old-fashioned vacuum tube can be replaced by the new 56. The radio circuit does not need to be changed at all. This new tube is very small, which can save space in the radio. The filament current is only 1 ampere, which is 75 amperes less than the 227, so it is especially suitable for radios with poor power transformers. Or, if you want to increase the number of vacuum tubes in your radio, using this new tube will not require any changes to the power section. 224丨丨 This vacuum tube can be replaced by 57 or 58. Sometimes, the primary of the high-frequency transformer needs to be replaced with one with a higher impedance, otherwise the efficiency will be poor. If using 57, the volume control must be reconnected in the cathode circuit instead of the screen circuit. The vacuum tube socket must be changed to a six-pin one. Replacing with this new tube can greatly improve the efficiency, whether it is detection or amplification. Saving filament current is the same as mentioned above.

288丨丨 This full-wave rectifier tube can be replaced by the new mercury vapor tube 82. The filament voltage must be changed to 2.5 volts. The advantage is that the voltage drop of this tube is only fifteen volts, so the output DC voltage can be increased. This increased voltage can increase the volume of the radio. The vacuum tube socket does not need to be changed, but a small high-frequency choke coil must be placed in the center connector of the high-voltage coil of the power transformer to eliminate the high-frequency current from flowing into the power section.

Application of Volume Control on Broadcasting Machines 218

— Luo Jingyu

Usually, we call a resistor made of German silver wire a Rheostat (variable resistor). Its purpose is mostly to control the current of the filament. There is another type, which is shaped like a variable resistor, and changes its value by moving a finger arm; however, the place where the finger arm is attached is not German silver wire, but raw materials such as carbon essence; called a Potentiometer or Volume grad (volume controller). As for the difference in their numerical values, the variable resistor is usually only a few tens of ohms; the volume controller is often from tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands.

The usual purpose of a volume controller is to be placed inside a radio to adjust the overload; First picture

Because a radio receives a local radio station, it obtains strong power due to the close distance, causing the received sound to be distorted. The volume controller used to remedy this phenomenon is sometimes used in the radio frequency amplification stage (such as ABC in the first figure), and sometimes in the audio frequency amplification stage (such as D in the figure). As for the comparison of resistance content numbers, it is often a hundred thousand ohms for the radio frequency amplification stage, and often five hundred thousand ohms for the audio frequency amplification stage.

There is another use here, which is to install it on the broadcasting machine to replace the switch. Suppose our broadcasting machine currently has three major parts: speech amplification stage, power amplification stage, and amplitude modulation stage. The microphone (Microphone) is connected to the speech amplification stage, specially for reports on the broadcasting station. The pickup (Pickup) is connected to the grid of the power amplification stage vacuum tube, specially for broadcasting gramophone music. In addition, there is a speech amplification stage connected from another concert hall, specially for broadcasting the performance program of that concert hall to radio listeners with radios. Then the control design is as shown in the second figure:

Second country

In the figure, A, B, and C are three volume controllers; if we only need report programs at this moment, then the arrow in A is moved from point D to point A, the arrow in B is moved to point B, and the arrow in C is moved to point F. This means that when the arrow in A is at point B, its circuit is short-circuited; now it is moved to point A, and there is a high resistance of tens of thousands of ohms between the two lines, so the current flows along the two lines to points 13. These two points are connected to the primary of the power amplification stage transformer. As for moving parts B and C to points D and F, it is just to make them short-circuited. Therefore, at this time, only report programs etc. are in the power amplification part. The low-frequency records or music from the concert hall will not seep in. On the contrary, if we only want the low-frequency music coming from the gramophone through the pickup to enter points 23 to the grid of the power amplification part, then move point A of part A to point B, and leave the arrow of part C on point F, and there will be absolutely no seepage effect. Because when part A is moved from point A to point B, it becomes short-circuited again. In the figure, the other two resistors control the power to the power amplification grid.

This design has two benefits for broadcasting machines: 1. Unlike using a switch for replacement, which has a popping sound that enters the ears of the listener, because it rotates the finger arm of the volume controller, gradually from zero to the maximum ohm value. 2. If we want to have an artistic taste when we report and adjust the monotony of our speech, we may still have a low-volume music as accompaniment, then in addition to short-circuiting part C in the figure, the pickup of part B is still moved to the rotating gramophone: just move the arrow on the volume regulator to a place with a considerable resistance value and not let it reach point D and become short-circuited, then we can hear the reporter's speech and the gramophone music at the same time. (The appropriate position of the finger arm determines the size of the resistance, the size of the resistance determines the business height of the gramophone music; as long as you experiment a little, the adjustment is extremely obedient and can achieve good results.

Another thing to note is that the screws on the finger arm of the volume controller will inevitably loosen after being turned for a long time. After loosening, the speech music broadcast will seep with firecracker sounds. If we occasionally ignore this reason, we will waste a lot of energy repeatedly investigating other parts and get no results. The author has been fooled by this, so I will add it here.

Travel-Type Super-Regeneration Radio in a Cigar Box 219

— Yi Sun

In travel-type wireless radios, the most important conditions are to make the mechanism simple and the weight light and small. A simple mechanism makes management very easy when in use, and light and small weight means that when climbing mountains or marching, carrying it with you is neither space-consuming nor labor-intensive. However, in addition to the above two main points, travel-type radios also need good volume, which is usually not easy to achieve. Now let me introduce a radio, the circuit of which can be seen in the first figure. This kind of radio weighs only three pounds without headphones, and because it is made in a cigar box, it occupies a very small place. Ordinary broadcast radio waves can be received, and what is even more wonderful is that it does not use the earth and sky lines (the antenna coil is wrapped around the edge of the box), so the selectivity is also good. When listening in Shanghai, Nanjing, Hangzhou, etc., it is clear and loud, without any noise.

This kind of super-regeneration

The power of the radio is particularly good. What is even stranger is that the B power only uses four and a half volts. According to actual testing, four and a half volts is enough for you to enjoy it. If there is no B battery, you can also receive radio, but the volume is too small. As you can see in the figure, because the Colpitts Interrupted Frequency Oscillator is used, the space occupied is reduced. The coils are adjusted with split nails, avoiding the trouble of moving coils and increasing the stability of radio reception. The choke coil is made of soft iron sheets one inch thick, two and a half inches long, and one inch wide. Thirty-five American standard enameled wires are enough to wrap around the core for five thousand turns, or you can buy a thirty Henry low-frequency choke coil.
