Antenna System to Eliminate Noise 220

— Xiang

When listening to beautiful music, the most annoying thing is the disturbance of noise; although some of the sources of noise are due to inevitable atmospheric electricity, most of them are man-made, such as the brightness of neon lights, the movement of trams, etc., which can all make the radio feel noise; what collects these many noises is not the antenna itself, but its accessories, the lead-in wire, so to eliminate noise, you only need to improve the installation of the lead-in wire, which is very effective.

First erect an antenna that is one hundred feet long, with a height of at least six feet above the roof, the higher the better; then make an antenna coupling transformer LI yourself: the winding method is to use a thirty-gauge double-layered yarn-wrapped wire, and wind it in overlapping layers for one hundred and fifty turns on a half-inch square wooden core. The width of the entire coil is 1/4 inch, and a connector is placed at the twenty-fifth turn: the inner end is grounded and the outer end is connected to the antenna; the lead-in wire must use a single wire with metal isolation (i.e., shielding Shield), one end is connected to the connector of L, and the other end is connected to the radio transformer L2. The manufacturing method of L2 is exactly the same as that of LI, except that one end must be

Series a 25ommF

Metal Isolation of Radio Antenna Lead-In Wire 221

Fixed capacitor, and then connect it to the antenna post of the radio; coils LILI should be immersed in a metal isolation box filled with wax. All metal isolators must be connected to the ground wire to be effective.

Using this kind of antenna device, the test results show that roughly eighty percent of the noise can be completely avoided, and the sensitivity and selectivity of the radio can also be improved a lot.

Small Experience 222

— Li Yuanqing

Two Methods of Winding Coils

It is usually difficult to make hand-wound coils neat and tight. Here are two methods that can achieve the above purpose:

Iron Nail Spring Copper Wire Iron Pliers 223

1. An iron nail is inserted into the spring, passed through the wooden tube, and clamped with iron pliers. (See figure) When winding the coil, the copper wire can be automatically withdrawn.

2. If the copper wire used is not the entire pound, then you can tie one end of the copper wire to the window hook, and when winding, people can move from far to near, and good results can also be obtained.

How to Avoid Body Capacity 224

When adjusting the radio, the sound is very loud, but when you let go, it is silent. This is because the human body has a capacitive effect on the radio. If the adjuster is a capacitor, you only need to connect its piece to the ground wire to avoid it. For other adjusters, you only need to lay a square copper sheet behind the adjustment handle, and then connect the copper sheet to the ground wire.

Calculation of Power Consumption of AC Radio 225

— Cheng Quan

Although AC radios consume very little electricity, most people lack basic electrical knowledge. Therefore, seeing the many tubes inside the machine and the loud sound, they assume it must be expensive to operate, and dare not use it freely. Some, renting rooms in other people's homes, cannot use it because the landlord is unclear, making it difficult to voice their grievances and feeling quite inconvenienced. In fact, AC radios consume very little electricity. The following two methods can be used to calculate the consumption. Radio owners who do a calculation will have confidence when using it. Those renting in other people's homes can also use it to calculate the exact amount of electricity consumed, which is convenient for both parties.

(1) On the back of an AC radio, there is a small copper plate with the machine's model number, the manufacturer's name, and the wattage consumed per hour. Suppose a certain radio consumes 100 watts per hour. Then, using it for ten hours consumes one kilowatt-hour (commonly known as "one unit," because the meter advancing one unit corresponds to a consumption of 1000 watts). A typical eight-tube, six-circuit radio consumes about 100 watts per hour. If the electricity cost is 16 cents per kilowatt-hour, then using it for one hour costs less than two cents of a silver dollar, which is extremely cheap.

(2) For self-made radios or other electrical appliances, the speed of the rotating wheel inside the meter's small window can be used to estimate consumption. If a certain radio, when in use, causes the meter's wheel to rotate 20 times per minute, then it rotates 1200 times per hour. Then, look at the number of rotations per kilowatt-hour (i.e., 1000 watts, or one unit) marked on the meter. Suppose the meter states:

1 KWH = 7500 REV·of Disc, which means one kilowatt-hour is consumed when the wheel rotates 7500 times. Now, if a certain radio makes the wheel rotate 1200 times per hour, then it consumes only 1200/7500 = 0.16 kilowatt-hours per hour (during the above test, the lights must be turned off, otherwise the result will be inaccurate).

Radio Receivers in the Plum Rain Season: The most vulnerable time for radio receivers is the plum rain season. With continuous drizzle, cloudy skies, and uncertain weather, the inside of the radio is easily affected by moisture. Circuit components either become moldy and rot or fall off. The most important parts are the resonant circuit coils. The square-frame circuits become moldy, or the resistors and capacitors corrode. As a result, the radio may produce strange noises or become completely silent, as well as various other inaudible phenomena. The radio repair department of Yada Company, located at No. 25 Renji Road in this city, has received a very large number of radio repair requests due to the continuous plum rain. They are currently hiring specialists to handle the repairs and ensure quick delivery. The company is also praised by all sectors for its low prices and perfect repairs.

Spring and Autumn

Talking While Picking Lice 227

— Zhan Lu

"A pheasant world, a lice-ridden building." Is this the opening warning line in a commoner's "Shanghai Ode"? Just eight words, both apt and poignant, give it the value to be passed down to this day.

It's getting hot; the ticks are raising their heads. Alas, this little thing has many names. Moreover, they are mostly recorded in books:

First, there's the tick. Second, there's the [unclear]. Third, there's the bedbug. Fourth, there's the "rich bug." Fifth, there's the stink bug. If the tick were to print business cards, it would already have so many cumbersome titles. But, looking in books, the tick has many, many more names.

Sixth, there's the [unclear]. Seventh, there's the flat tick, as the "Shandu Si Kao" says. Eighth, there's the wood tick, as the "Wu Za Zu" describes. Ninth, there's the [unclear], as the "Shi Wu Yuan Zhu" says. Tenth, there's the [unclear]. Eleventh, there's the wall flea, as the "Liu Shu Gu" says. The tick has even crossed the ocean, and the Japanese call it the Nanjing bug. This is the tick's twelfth fragrant name.

Some say that calling the tick the Nanjing bug is the Japanese intentionally insulting China, because ticks are not a product of Nanjing that is "the only one, with no branches." I say: how can the Nanjing bug be as fierce as the Japanese leech? The three words "Japanese leech" are world-famous. Recently, in the streams along the Jinghu (Nanjing-Shanghai) railway line, there have been Japanese blood flukes. Alas! This is worth making us turn pale at the mention of bugs.

In the past, Wang Meng discussed affairs while picking lice, and the lice he picked were white lice. Of course, he could pick and talk. But, if a Shanghai resident living in a lice-ridden building wants to imitate Wang Meng and talk while picking lice, hey! If he doesn't pick, all is well. Once he picks, the stinking odor assaults his nostrils, and he doesn't even have time to spit. How can he talk? This is what people in Suzhou say: "Talking is not worth talking."

Ceaseless Flow 228

— Zui Chi Sheng

"Ceaseless flow" is a common saying, and also an auspicious phrase to solicit good fortune. All people engaged in business hope their business will be prosperous, with "ceaseless flow." Therefore, merchants write these four characters on their signboards and in their account books, expressing their hopes.

Unexpectedly, today, this phrase is being applied to the "Sichuan War," and has almost become an "unlucky term." Clearly interpreting the literal meaning, it means "The war in Sichuan flows ceaselessly in rotation." It's laughable. Since the founding of the Republic of China, our country has seen domestic wars rising and falling, truly a ceaseless flow. Especially Sichuan Province, for more than ten years, the wars have been cyclical, repeated countless times. Recently, the struggle between the two Lius has caused immense suffering. Now, before the wounds have healed, Generals Deng and Liu are fighting again. With wars flowing ceaselessly like this, how can the people bear it? How can the country survive?

At this critical time of national crisis, the high-ranking commanding officers and senior military officials have such great interest, expending unusual effort, and engaging in a major fight. They are not afraid of the people booing, and not afraid of foreigners laughing their teeth off. I truly admire their deep cultivation. Although the central government has issued repeated orders and telegrams, trying to stop them, these people's excitement is at its peak, and the war is in full swing. They are not willing to stop for a while. It's like siblings fighting in a family, beating each other until their heads are bleeding, and the parents' calls to stop are ineffective. Is this still a family? This is precisely what the enemy calls "an unorganized country."

Alas... the ceaseless bloodshed in Sichuan, the impact of which will cause the entire country to "suffer the consequences."

New Swindling Tricks Using Telegrams 229

— Cheng Zhi Zheng

Recently, swindling tricks in Europe and America have become increasingly bizarre. Some even use telegrams to defraud large sums of money, making it impossible to guard against. As a result, news of victims is heard daily. Here is one example:

Miss Jane Doe is the private secretary of a certain wealthy merchant. The wealthy merchant was traveling overseas. One day, the lady received a telegram from him. The location of the telegram's origin was the European city he was scheduled to arrive in. The telegram read: "Pay attention to the goods sent by Kara. Do not pay more than 1500 yuan. This matter must be kept absolutely secret. Wait for me to return before opening." It was signed with his name. Within a few days, a person claiming to be Kara contacted Miss Joan Doe by phone and soon sent a large box, claiming that it contained famous wine and tax-evading carpets. Miss Joan Doe immediately followed her master's telegram and paid 1500 yuan. After that, the so-called Kara disappeared without a trace. When the master returned and asked about it, he knew nothing about it. When the box was opened, it contained only some old wine and rags.

Telegraph bureaus and shipping companies have repeatedly asked all parties to take appropriate precautions against telegram scams. However, dozens of merchants have already been victimized. In New York City alone, criminal gangs swindled them out of $1,000,000 last year. The situation in other cities in the West is even worse. According to a recent New York newspaper report, fifteen accomplices have been arrested and are being rigorously interrogated, but there is still no progress. The remaining accomplices are still rampant. The president of a Chicago bank was also defrauded of $5,925. Their methods are extremely clever, often falsely claiming that the items being transported contain books, diamonds, famous carpets, famous wines, etc., asking for prices ranging from $400 to $40,000.

The gang seems to be a large organization, and they communicate with each other in various places. Their information is extremely sensitive. Each time a ship leaves the country, they try to copy the names of the people on board and find out their personalities and preferences, so that they can use tricks. Currently, shipping companies and telegraph companies are warning passengers to inform their relatives and friends not to be deceived.

Go Play in the Cold Water 230

— Rong Yu

In this hot weather, we see that clear water, as bright as glass. We also imagine the coolness of the water, which must be more pleasant than drinking soda and shaking an electric fan. We can't wait to plunge in and soak to our heart's content. But don't be reckless! If you can't swim, and if there is no one to guide you, that kind of jump, where the water splashes, are you not afraid to follow Qu Yuan and become a victim? Are you not afraid to learn from Li Xueshi, who jumped into the river to catch the moon and never returned? If you can't swim, no matter how great your ability is, you won't have any strength in the water. Haven't you seen "Water Margin"? Brother Black Whirlwind Li, his tolerance on land is so fierce. In the Xunyang River, he was immersed by the White Stripe in the Waves Zhang Shun until his eyes turned white, his stomach bloated, and he almost couldn't breathe. So I advise you to go play in the cold water, but if you can't swim, you must first learn some basic strokes.

For people in Shanghai who want to take a cold bath, the open-air swimming pool in Hongkou Park is the best. The water is so clean and there are no waves. In the sunset, girls wearing colorful clothes and attendants in Western suits, changed into swimsuits, paddling and playing in the water. Seeing it will make you jealous, "Only envy the mandarin ducks, not the immortals." I guarantee that people will have this feeling! It's a pity that the tickets are too expensive, one dollar for three. If you go to wash every day, it will cost you more than ten dollars a month!

There is also the Gaoqiao seaside resort, which is said to have been very well arranged since last year. It's a pity that I haven't been there to visit. However, from Shanghai to there, you have to take a boat and then a car, and you will be tired and sweaty on the road. You can only try it occasionally. It is really inconvenient to go every day!

Thirty years ago, in the summer, I was still studying in a private school. There was no summer vacation in the private school. When it was time to attend evening school, I felt dizzy and drowsy. I would invite some mischievous schoolmates to take a cold bath in the small river. Soaking our bodies in the water was like eating ginseng fruit. Every one of our thirty-six thousand pores felt happy. After bathing, we could still find crabs, snails, and clams on the riverbed. If we were lucky, we could also find eels and loaches in the holes beside the river. However, we always gave these things to others and never dared to take them home. Because the parents at that time were more stubborn than they are now. A shout would ask, "Do you dare to take a cold bath next time?" We young ones didn't dare to be stubborn, so we had to secretly wash outside.

The small river is a natural open-air swimming pool, always with some earthy smell and muddy taste, how can it be compared to artificial buildings. Modern men and women, seeing the green water, surrounded by countless small grasses, fish swimming, shrimp jumping, and if it is not just right, there are also water snakes swimming, how dare you jump down. Forget it: let this natural swimming pool be used by the village children!

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 231

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 8: Harsh Words Provoke a Young Man to Resign and Flee; A Kind-Hearted Girl Mercifully Escorts Her Relatives Here

Huang Manying had already heard from Company Commander Tian that Commander Zhao had a lover in mind, the Yang girl who lived in the same courtyard, presumably this was the girl. Women always like to talk about other people's love affairs with their lovers, and they also like to see other people's lovers. This is something that has nothing to do with them, but they find it interesting. Huang Manying initially had the impulse of curiosity to talk to Gui Zhi. When they had been talking for a long time, she felt that Gui Zhi was also a very good person, so she opened the white cloth package. It was a gray silk vest and two pairs of wool socks. Huang Manying smiled and said, "This vest is filled with silk floss, which I sewed myself. I knitted half of these two pairs of wool socks myself, and asked someone else to knit the other half. These times, Company Commander Tian was busy with affairs in the camp because the road to the city was far, so he didn't succeed in going. He wrote me a letter, teaching me to deliver it to Commander Zhao's house. It's just that he didn't make an appointment, so I don't know what day is best to send it. Therefore, I rushed to get the things done, and ran over today. As for running into an empty house, I didn't expect it." Gui Zhi said, "Were these all done by Miss Huang and Company Commander Tian?" Huang Manying, hearing these words, felt a little inconvenient to answer directly, and just smiled as she reached out to adjust her hair. Gui Zhi said, "It doesn't matter, you put it down, and we will give it to Commander Zhao, and this will be transferred to Company Commander Tian's hands. We know that these are important things, and we will definitely not break them." Huang Manying laughed: "If you say that, I would be too stingy. These things can't be pinched off a piece, or bitten off a piece, so what am I worried about." As she spoke, she rolled up the package, put it on the kang, and got up as if she was about to leave. Gui Zhi suddenly exclaimed, "Oh! Miss Huang, you can't leave. It's too late to go into the city now." Huang Manying said, "Why? Is the city gate closed this early?" Gui Zhi said: "The long-distance bus passed by at four thirty, this time, it's five o'clock. If you take a rickshaw into the city, it will be dark on the way." Aunt Jiang said: "Yes! It gets dark early now, and it is a bit inconvenient for a young lady to be out alone." (95)

Silk and Tea

Cocoon Market Nearing its End 245

(Pinghu Cocoon Business Has Ceased Weighing) This year's cocoon production is only about 40-50%. Only a dozen or so cocoon businesses opened, and the amount of cocoons collected was insufficient. Farmers' silkworm costs were not low, so they insisted on high prices before selling. As a result, many people in Nan Shuanglin and other places spun their own silk. Cocoon businesses have all stopped weighing. The highest price for improved variety cocoons was 55 yuan, and the lowest price for native cocoons was 25 yuan.

(Danyang New Cocoon Production Quite Abundant) Farmers who raised improved varieties accounted for 80%. The silkworm season was quite good, with the new cocoon harvest about 80% of a normal year. The quality of the cocoons was also excellent. Cocoon businesses competed to buy high-quality cocoons, with the highest price being 50 yuan and the lowest being 28 yuan. The average price was 32-33 yuan. Cocoon businesses have stopped buying.

(Changzhou Cocoon Businesses Mostly Stopped Buying) Cocoon production averaged 70-80%. Many people in the eastern countryside raised foreign varieties, so the cocoons were of better quality. Cocoon businesses opened for over a week, and the amount of cocoons collected was not small. Most have stopped buying. The price of cocoons was highest for foreign varieties, with private deals in the eastern countryside reaching 60 yuan. When goods arrived, the price returned to 50 yuan on weighing day. Native cocoons were 35-36 yuan.

(Dongting Mountain Cocoon Production Only 50%) This year, farmers in the eastern and western mountains of Dongting were economically impoverished, so the amount of cocoons raised was reduced. Cocoon production was only about 50% of previous years. Improved variety cocoons were 60 yuan per load (Sima weight), and native cocoons were 34 yuan per load.

(Artificial Silk Sales Not Quiet) Yesterday, merchants from Chang'an, Haining, and other places brought 38 cases of June futures contracts for brands such as Lady Junzi and DPS Shijintu, with prices ranging from 167.15 yuan to 155.25 yuan net.

(Silk Merchant) New York silk prices continued to rise. Raw silk has risen by one dollar and ninety cents. Silk is also very popular. White factory spun silk sold 500 bales, white dry spun silk 160 bales, yellow factory spun silk 100 bales, Sichuan factory spun silk 12 bales, and coarse yellow silk 13 bales.

Tunxi Fine Eyebrow Tea Exports Improve 246

Yesterday, the Jardine Matheson, Xiehe, Tongfu, Tianyu, and other firms dealing in Gao Zhuang Fine Eyebrow Green Tea all received responses to their telegrams sent in previous days, so they all began to take action. The price of Gongxi tea from the eastern Wuyuan area had already opened at 150 yuan. Gao Zhuang goods sold well. In addition, Zhucha and other varieties of tea from local estates, as well as Needle Eyebrow and Beautiful Eyebrow teas from mountain estates, all had lively sales routes. Green tea had slightly improved. Although there was no significant development in Qimen Black Tea, sales prices had fallen to their lowest point, and exchange rates had eased in recent days, making prices more affordable. As a result, Jardine Matheson resumed operations, and the market was more lively than yesterday.

Qimen Tea Merchants Request a Change in the Weights and Measures System 247

The Qimen Tea Industry Association pointed out that the government had long issued orders to implement the kilogram system for weights and measures, but foreign firms exporting tea still used the pound system, resulting in significant losses for merchants. It has been reported that they have telegraphed the Shanghai Foreign Firm Tea Industry Association to request a correction in order to respect the law and protect the interests of merchants.

Grain and Rice Market Retail Sales Dull 248

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the source was 30-40 ships, and the outbound traffic was slightly lower. However, sellers tried their best to boost sales due to the cloudy weather. However, due to limited outbound traffic, only Suzhou japonica rice increased slightly, while other varieties such as Changbang and Lianggang japonica rice, Tianjin and Weihaiwei varieties, and 1,000 odd bags of office rice remained unchanged. Qingjiao, Songjiang, Sixi, Lian and other thin rice varieties were all stable. There was no major change in the market. Only Yinyuan rice sold slightly better, and the Shanghai price was stable. Bianyuan rice did not change.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were about 17-18 ships from various routes along the river. Although the wholesale of white japonica rice was not strong, the market was brisk due to the cloudy weather and the willingness to buy. The market was stable and slightly higher, with prices firm. The arrival of early thin rice was smooth and prices were stable. There were few arrivals of Yangjian rice, and the outbound traffic continued, with prices remaining tight by several points. Dubu kejian and Yinbianyuan rice were stable.

Wenzhou and Taizhou Merchants Continue to Buy Foreign Indica Rice 249

(Hunan and Jiangxi Indica Rice and Foreign Wheat Continue to be Small)

Yesterday, there were continued arrivals of Indica rice, although in small quantities. In addition to Hunan and Jiangxi Indica rice, Anhui, Nanjing, and Jiangbei varieties were also loaded. Sellers were eager to sell for cash, so the prices of Hunan and Jiangxi varieties continued to fall. There were fewer arrivals of Anhui, Jiangbei, and Nanjing varieties, and Wenzhou and Taizhou merchants inquired about them, so the market gradually recovered and increased by four or five points yesterday. Small machine-ground foreign rice also fell by five points. Wenzhou, Taizhou, and Fujian merchants bought Hunan and Jiangxi rice, and the other mixed varieties were bought by Wenzhou and Taizhou merchants. Wenzhou and Taizhou appetite increased, while Fujian appetite was slightly lower, so the amount of outbound traffic was similar. Daily transactions included 186 bags of Jiangxi machine-ground late rice at 8.26 yuan, 800 bags of Hunan machine-ground oil rice at 8.5 yuan, 450 bags of Qiyou rice at 7.3 yuan, 753 bags of Nanlu rough rice at 6.65 yuan, and Jiangbei machine-ground Indica rice at 7.4 yuan. Small machine-ground rice was priced at 7.75 yuan, and the prices of secondary grades also fell.

Flour and Wheat Decline in the Morning, Recover in the Afternoon 250

After the market opened in the morning, foreign wheat prices rose slightly. The flour merchants jointly requested that the authorities postpone the shipment of American wheat, which was already loaned, for half a year to help the people of Jiangsu and provide a livelihood for the farmers who depend on new wheat. The factories believed that flour prices were already low, making it unprofitable to sell further, and hoped that the authorities would approve the request to delay the shipment of American wheat to China, which would turn the market around. Therefore, they unanimously sold, and the northern merchants, who had an appetite for flour, immediately rushed to buy and load. Shorts and speculators also tried their best to buy and cover, and futures flour was particularly absorbed by small investors, so the price gradually improved. The market improved even further in the afternoon, with closing prices higher: June/July up 1.25, August up 1, September up 1.75, and October/November up 2.25.

The wheat market continued the previous day's decline in the morning, and merchants sold even more aggressively. More wheat from producing areas was sold, and prices continued to fall sharply, with distant months down by 4-5 points and nearby months down by 1-3 points. In the afternoon, due to the request to delay the shipment of American wheat, sentiment stabilized, and factories competed to buy. Shorts covered, and prices suddenly rebounded by 5, 6, 7, or 8 points. As a result, prices rose by 2, 3, or 4 points. 200 bags of new wheat from Wujiang were opened, and the price remained at 4 yuan. With fewer arrivals, the market outlook was positive.

Soybean Oil and Cake Market Listless 251

Soybean oil demand from various regions was weak, so market sentiment turned soft, but merchants were still firm in their intentions. However, peanut oil prices were stable due to the scarcity of arrivals and stocks. Soybean cake demand has been sluggish recently, and the market is temporarily in a holding pattern. Vehicle beans once rebounded, but were affected by continuous declines, and saw a slight correction of 3-4 points. Sales of other beans were also low, and the market remained stable.

New North Goods, Wood Ear Fungus, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 252

After the first batch of new wood ear fungus arrived in Hankou, merchants from Guangdong directly purchased most of it, and Shanghai merchants also purchased some. It was reported yesterday that the goods purchased by Shanghai merchants had arrived by Ningbo and Shaoxing ships, with an approximate wholesale price of 77 yuan. Samples will be available for viewing today.

Five Metals, White Lead Sheets, Five or Six Hundred Barrels Arrived Yesterday 253

(Some Tin also Arrived)

White lead sheets, which had been out of stock for many days, arrived yesterday from England, with 500-600 barrels unloaded at the Huashun Wharf. The prices of 80-90 grades were quite good, selling for 24 taels, while the price of No. 2 was very weak due to the scarcity of supply to Guangzhou. It was reported that it only sold for 24 taels and 5 qian per dan, which was more than one tael lower than before. In addition, there were few changes in other colors.

Tin, which had been out of stock for many days, arrived in new shipments yesterday at Swire Warehouse, Jinliyuan Wharf, etc. There was no fear of a shortage of goods on the market, and the price was unchanged from the previous day.

Survey of Shanghai Cost of Living Index for Last Month 254

Kerosene Continues to Fall, Firewood Weak

Food and Miscellaneous Items Both Rise

The Tariff Commission recently published the Shanghai Cost of Living Index, which stated: "The Shanghai Cost of Living Index compiled by the Commission for May 1933 was 106.8, an increase of 0.5% compared to the previous month and a decrease of 9.1% compared to the same month last year. In the fuel category, kerosene continued to fall and firewood weakened, so the index fell sharply by 7.4% compared to the previous month. However, due to the larger weight of the food category index, which rose by 0.9%, and the miscellaneous category index, which rose by 2.5%, the resulting overall index still rose slightly. The various category indexes are compared in the table below."

Free Talk

Ode to the Night 255

— You Guang

Those who love the night are not only the lonely, the idle, the incapable of fighting, the afraid of light.

People's conduct, both in the daytime and in the deep of night, under the sun and before the lamp, often appears different. Night is the profound celestial robe woven by nature, universally covering all people, making them warm and secure, unknowingly gradually shedding their man-made masks and garments, nakedly wrapped in this boundless, black fluff-like mass.

Though it is night, there is also light and darkness. There is dim light, there is gloom, there is reaching out and not seeing one's palm, there is pitch-black chaos. Those who love the night must have ears to hear the night and eyes to see the night, freely seeing all darkness in the dark. Gentlemen walk from under the electric light into a dark room, stretching their lazy waists; lovers walk from under the moonlight into the shade of trees, suddenly changing their expressions. The arrival of night obliterates all the transcendence, unity, vagueness, suddenness, and brilliance written by men of letters and scholars on dazzling white paper in the light of day, leaving only the nightly air of begging, pleasing, lying, deceiving, boasting, and playing tricks, forming a brilliant golden halo, like that seen in Buddhist paintings, enveloping the heads of extraordinary learning.

Those who love the night then receive the light given by the night.

The high-heeled modern girl walks vigorously on the street under the electric light, but a little oily sweat also sparkles on her nose, proving that she is a beginner in fashion. If she were grown in bright illumination, she would encounter the fate of "decline." The darkness of a long row of stores helps her, allowing her to slow down the full horsepower and take a breath, at which point she feels the refreshing cool breeze in the night.

Those who love the night and the modern girl then simultaneously receive the grace given by the night.

One night has ended, and people carefully get up and come out again, and the faces of the couples are so different from five or six o'clock before. From then on, there is liveliness and clamor. But behind high walls, in the middle of tall buildings, in deep boudoirs, in black prisons, in guest rooms, in secret agencies, a startling, true, great darkness still pervades.

The current bright daylight, with its bustling crowds, is the decoration of this darkness, the golden lid on the jar of human flesh sauce, the snow cream on the ghost face. Only the night is still honest. I love the night, and in the night, I compose an "Ode to the Night."

Dilemma 256

— Cao Juren

Ji Yun's "Notes from the Cottage of Close Observation" records that a certain widow took her orphaned son and her elderly aunt to flee and cross a river. The current was very rapid. In the middle of the river, the elderly aunt was swept into the water. The widow hurriedly put her orphaned son aside to rescue her elderly aunt. Who knew that after rescuing her elderly aunt, she lost her orphaned son. The old woman, having saved her old life, rebuked the widow, saying, "What is the use of my old life? The only bloodline of a certain family is this orphan! Now that the orphan is lost, what is the use of my old life!" But if the widow had held her orphaned son and ignored her elderly aunt, others would surely rebuke, "This kind of woman is too heartless! She only loves her own son and doesn't even care about her mother-in-law!" Ji Yun said it well: in the middle of the river, the situation was critical. Putting the son down and rushing to save her mother-in-law, there was no time to think. It was truly not easy for a certain widow to be a person. "Straight" brought rebuke, and "horizontal" also brought rebuke, leaving her with no way out!

Now, the position of a group of friends who wield pens is exactly the same as that of a certain widow. If you want to offer loyal advice or criticize the current situation, some will say that you have an X or Y color, and that you have already eaten "radishes." If you change direction, not criticizing politics but criticizing society, others will laugh, "Are you talking about romance now! Hmph!" But if you change direction again, not criticizing politics or society, and praising the wise rule like others, will you escape praise and blame? Immediately, others will suspect that you want to steal their rice bowl and will gossip even more mercilessly. There is a Western story of a father and son riding a donkey. It was not good for both to ride, and it was not good for both not to ride. It was not good for the father to ride and the son to walk, and it was not good for the son to ride and the father to walk. Helpless, they had to lift the donkey together, both sweating profusely while carrying it, and the donkey didn't know where to complain. Today's literati truly find it difficult to be people no matter what they do!

George Bernard Shaw in Beiping and Tianjin 257

— Li Jinming

George Bernard Shaw was welcomed by the general public when he arrived in Shanghai, but he encountered indifference everywhere he went in Beiping and Tianjin. When the train he was riding arrived in Tianjin, a group of students who admired him came to the station to welcome him, holding a banner that read, "Welcome to Our Great George Bernard Shaw." Who would have thought that Shaw would not appreciate this flattery and slammed the window shut in front of the welcoming crowd. A journalist standing next to him said to him, "Have you arrived in Tianjin and you still don't know?" Shaw replied, "Tin and Zinc? Of course I know."

Shaw stated very early that he was coming to China to visit Beiping and the Great Wall. But when he arrived in Beiping, apart from "Young Marshal Zhang" arranging his residence, the educational and intellectual circles of Beiping and Tianjin were completely silent. Apart from carrying short news reports, the press was unusually disrespectful in their reviews of him. They all felt offended by Shaw's statement that "China has no culture to speak of," believing that Shaw used the same tone as that of satirizing Mrs. Warren and her priest to ridicule China, which was truly shameful. But in reality, Shaw came to China with good intentions. He felt that China did not have much culture, and this was probably also the truth that many Westerners saw. Which book published in London promotes Chinese culture?

Based on our speculation, there are approximately three reasons why the educational and intellectual circles of Beiping and Tianjin ignored Shaw. First, most people did not know who Shaw was. I remember that on the day before Shaw arrived in Beiping, a professor in the Department of Sinology at a certain university outside Heping Gate read the newspaper in the lounge and exclaimed in astonishment, "Hey, there are actually foreigners named Xiao?" This was widely told as a joke. Second, they were afraid of losing face. The intellectual circles of Beiping have always respected Plato's saying that "knowledge is virtue," and their cultivation is very deep and broad. They felt that Shaw did not have a gentlemanly demeanor at all, and that his opening remarks were "vicious sentences," so rather than embarrassing themselves by welcoming him, they chose to ignore him. Third, they were not of the same kind. If Bertrand Russell or John Dewey had gone to Beiping and Tianjin, even the directors of education and university presidents there would have had to come forward to shake hands with them. But Shaw was just a writer of humorous texts, and he was really not qualified enough. This kind of psychology is just like that of Forgthe described by Shaw's comrade John Galsworthy in "The Man of Property," "suspicion for the wise, contempt for the artist." Therefore, the educational circles of Beiping (not referring to the entire group) only knew how to ensure the safety of their salaries, and how to open shops in the name of righteousness after receiving their salaries (but they were not pure at heart). In return for the cold treatment that Shaw received in Beiping, they only expressed the insensitivity of a group of corrupt elements. No wonder he went to Japan and the first thing he did was to meet with Marshal Araki.

Seven Days in a Hospital Bed (Continued) 258

— Ms. Xiong Xiang

May 22nd

The person from Shaoxing in the room is the most interesting, always talking and laughing. What she says often makes everyone in the room unable to stop themselves from smiling, forgetting their illness. She refuses to tell the truth about her life. Judging by her demeanor, she is not someone who can forget her worries, but she is very happy. The woman from Hubei eloped with a man and severed ties with her parents. Life hasn't been good since she left, and she often covers her face in the bed and sobs. She looks like a thirteen or fourteen-year-old girl, but her heart has already experienced hardship. The woman from Jiangxi is a large woman. Her husband works in a factory and never has time to visit her. I heard that he can only earn forty cents a day, but the third-class ward costs fifty cents. The woman from Guangdong seems to have a better family situation, but she lies in bed all day without saying a word.

Today I discovered that the Jiangxi woman doesn't have enough vegetables. She can only be half full at each meal. I gave her my portion because Ming-ge had sent me extra vegetables. The hospital's vegetables are only in two thin small dishes. I don't know if they are afraid that the patients will get sick from eating too much, or if people in the third-class ward should eat less.

Ming-ge looked at my diary and seemed unhappy. I knew it was because my dream the night before touched his hidden feelings. That dream is truly cursed. But it's like a night owl, attacking my heart, impossible to get rid of. I also know that I shouldn't have had that dream. Lian-sheng is the night owl, isn't Ming-ge my loud rooster crowing at dawn? I want to face the dawn and never return to the darkness. Goodbye, Lian-sheng? I don't want to dream of you again.

May 22nd

The Jiangxi woman didn't pay her bill. The doctor said that hospitalization costs money and they can't do charity, so she had to move out. The Shaoxing woman also left in the afternoon. The Guangdong woman had surgery. Now that the surgery has healed, she is being moved to the internal medicine department. Only the newcomer and I are left here. The woman from Hubei paid two dollars. She calculated it several times and said that she had already stayed for several days and couldn't stay any longer, and her illness was not getting better, so she was very anxious. I had prepaid seven dollars, so I was considered to have the best situation among them and could stay for fourteen days. The regulation is that the third-class ward requires a fifteen-dollar prepayment, but no one in the third class has that kind of ability. It shows what kind of people are in the third-class ward. This hospital is not doing charity.

In the afternoon, the Hubei woman asked the tea boy to go to the accounting office to calculate the bill and wrote a letter to the doctor requesting a fee reduction. It is unknown what the result was. She immediately got dressed and went out. Soon another newcomer came in, so the room was still just the newcomer and me. Ming-ge sent a lot of food again today. (To be continued)

Carrot Top 259

— By Jules Renard, translated by Lin Qu

Mathilde

"Mama, do you know?" Sister Ernestine came running to Mrs. Lepic, breathless. "Carrot Top and little Mathilde are pretending to be husband and wife in the pasture. Brother Felix is dressing them up. I remember you said we weren't allowed to do this, if I remember correctly."

Indeed, little Mathilde stood motionless in the pasture, adorned with wild clematis vines with white flowers. She was dressed up so colorfully, she looked like a real bride decorated with orange blossoms. She also had something to ease all the pain of life.

The clematis vines on her body were initially woven into a circle worn on her head, and then hung down one by one, under her chin, on her back, on both arms, curling around her body, all the way to the ground, dragging into a tail. Brother Felix also tried his best to lengthen this tail.

He stepped back a few paces and said:

"Don't move! Now it's your turn, Carrot Top."

Now it was Carrot Top's turn to dress up as a young groom. He was also covered in clematis vines, dotted here and there with poppies, dandelions, hawthorns, etc., to make him look different from Mathilde. He didn't mean to smile; all three of them looked very serious. They knew the attitude to take in every kind of ceremony. Participating in a funeral should always look sad; participating in a wedding should remain solemn before the end of the mass. Otherwise, playing would be no fun.

"You have to hold hands," Brother Felix said. "Go forward! Don't be too fast."

The two of them stood loosely side by side, keeping pace as they walked forward. When Mathilde found it difficult to walk, she rolled up the long train made of clematis vines and held it in her hand. Carrot Top waited for her obediently, raising one leg, making a stepping motion.

Brother Felix led them through the pasture. He walked backwards in front of them, swinging his arms, so that they wouldn't mess up their steps. He first pretended to be the mayor saluting them, then pretended to be the priest blessing them, then pretended to be the congratulatory guests praising them, and finally pretended to be the musician rubbing one stick against another to represent a violin.

He made them walk crisscross.

"Stop!" he said. "Now it's messed up."

He smoothed the flower crown on Mathilde's head and then called them to walk again.

"Ah-yi!" Mathilde cried out in a strange way.

A tendril on the clematis vine hooked her hair. Brother Felix tore it all off for her. Everyone continued walking. "Okay," he said, "Now you're married, you can kiss."

He saw them hesitating and said:

"What! What are you afraid of! Kiss. People should kiss when they get married. Make some flattering gestures and say some words of love. Your faces all look like they're wrapped in lead."

He who was better and perhaps already talked about love, laughed at their clumsiness. He first kissed Mathilde - this was his reward for his hard work - setting an example for them.

Carrot Top mustered his courage and, through the tangled plants, sought Mathilde's face, and he kissed her on the cheek.

"This isn't a joke," he said. "I will really marry you in the future."

Mathilde also returned a kiss on Carrot Top's cheek. Immediately, clumsy, awkward, both of them blushed.

Brother Felix made fun of them.

"Blushing! Blushing!"

He rubbed two fingers together, stomped his feet, and had a slight mocking smile on his lips. (To be continued)

Talk

The Night Soil Master 260

— Geng

When I read Yu Chengde of the Qing Dynasty saying, "Truly know the city people are cunning, not as good as the country people foolish, the country people regard rice as pearls and jade, the granary officials trample it like mud," I can't help but deeply feel that the life of city people has been superior to that of country people since ancient times, and the country people's cherishing of material resources is far beyond what the profligate city people can compare to. Is there anything more unfair in the world than this?

Little did I know that with the changes in the world and even reaching the current world that advocates people's livelihood, country people who see rice as pearls and firewood as cassia are everywhere, and city people who cherish food and drink, even to the point of shedding blood to protect their rights to night soil, have also been found in Wenzhou.

According to reports, the total annual income from night soil in Wenzhou is more than 200,000 yuan. Now, due to the shortage of educational funds, there is a proposal to nationalize night soil. The citizens, with the overwhelming reason that "the tax donations of the four major elements of democracy have already exceeded twice the original price, and there is no food to eat, so where does the night soil come from," unanimously opposed it, and it even developed into a bloody incident (excerpt from a Wenzhou dispatch from a certain newspaper).

This news, compared to the strange incident in Sichuan where grain taxes have been collected until the 63rd year of the Republic of China, makes me feel that although their methods and designs are different, their intention to kill the goose to get the eggs can be eternally bound by a thousand miles of spiritual communion!

If the donations and taxes paid before, which were so-called "more than twice the original price," were indeed returned to the public and used properly, the small amount of educational expenses would not have fallen under the category of having no source. If it is absolutely necessary to do so, as long as the nationalized night soil is truly used to cover educational expenses, then even if the people fart, they will prepare to publicly create "ammonia," and who would say that it shouldn't be?

"Treating the sore in front of your eyes, cutting out the flesh from your heart," the parties involved repeatedly chant, and they will not know where the tears will come from!

To My Wei 261

— Liang

My beloved Wei… Since your disappearance on April 30th, I have been in a state of extreme confusion and madness, and endless grief has been tearing at my soul. I haven't had a single night of restful sleep, I haven't cried out in my dreams without a sound, I haven't forgotten you for a single moment. This uncontrollable, intense pain is more than ten thousand times harder for me to bear than the death penalty! You are everything in my life, your disappearance has destroyed my world! I can't live without you! My dear, come back!

For the past few years, our love has been so intimate for so long, so sweet and intense that everyone envied and praised us. We also showed off to all the lovers, our passionate embraces, our mad kisses, our… our vows to die together, our hugging and crying together, our mutual affection, all of this… is my steadfast belief in you. I will never believe that you would resolutely abandon me! I will never believe that you would heartlessly abandon me! Especially at this time when we have encountered misfortune? My dear, come back!

However, all the past joys have now become present sorrows. This heart of mine, this chest that you leaned on when you were shrouded in drowsy sleepiness, you can easily imagine the current grief and despair! But I would rather have the opportunity to open it up to you, so that you can seriously recognize that this is a heart that cannot be abandoned! My heart's desire is that you can find true happiness in the long journey of life, that you will not suffer the slightest bit of sorrow. I am willing to pay for this with all my bleeding and my entire life! Every thread of my thoughts is for you! My dear, come back!

My beloved, you have disappeared after all. More than a month after your disappearance, there is no news. After I asked many friends and lawyers to inquire and investigate everywhere, I know that you have not been implicated or arrested. In my pain, I can't help but think that you have been seduced by good people! Wei! This conjecture may be an insult to you, but now, in order to find out the truth about you, I have to make such a guess with tears of pain. Alas! My tears are pouring out like a tide! My dear, come back.

Wei, even if you have been deceived, I believe it is not your will. I think you had a momentary nervous breakdown. You may have lost your freedom now, because the flowers of sincere and pure love cannot be destroyed by any environment or material things! Please tell me, have you ever met anyone who cares for you as carefully as I do, in any place? How worried I was when you had a little illness! I swear, I love you more than I love my own life. My dear, come back.

There is an unspeakable pain in my heart. Because of your disappearance, I now feel that I have not fulfilled my responsibility for your education. Your momentary confusion, your momentary wavering, is entirely because I have not loved you enough. I hate myself, I will never blame you. If you can come back, I will love you even more in the future. Even if you are insulted by others and are pregnant, I will not blame you, be angry with you. I will still love you even more, giving my entire heart's desire, all the time in my life, to seek your happiness, because you are everything in my life, the whole entrustment of my life! These past thirty days have proved that I cannot leave you for a moment. Without you, I cannot live! These past thirty days! Intense grief has caused me to faint countless times! Wei, I now know that if a mortal has not fulfilled his heart's desire for the one he loves, his pain is worse than death. If you have abandoned me because I have not loved you enough, then how much more tragic is the pain in my heart? My dear, come back!

Alas, all our past, at this time, makes me think of it. I think of our little life, that lovely Lingzi. If she were still alive, she would already be calling you Mom and calling me Dad. She would also make you unable to bear to abandon us! Alas! I think even more about how you have been living your life in the past month or so in such a hot and tormented situation. Has your heart disease worsened? All of this breaks my heart! My beloved wife, you must not be deceived by vanity. That momentary passion is only a momentary impulse. Outsiders cannot be relied on. He will never truly love you. When he gets tired of you, he will abandon you. The vision of this ending is extremely miserable! Have you not thought about it, who has ever truly loved a married woman? It's just that they see you as young now, or they are cheating you into selling it. You don't see the darkness of Shanghai society in the newspapers? When I think of this, my heart is like a knife, I grieve for you, I dare not think about it! My dear, if you continue like this, how can you see your mother? The mother who is always thinking of you, that old and frail mother? My dear, come back!

Since we came together, the arduous journey is worth cherishing, and our everlasting love is worth praising.

Page 22

Now I only hate myself. The mistake that caused this incident was entirely my own. If I hadn't let you go to work this spring, there would never have been the tragic situation now. It was entirely that bad environment that corrupted you. Alas, my love, let me see you, and from now on I will never let you go to work again. I will exhaust my heart and mind to atone for my past mistakes! My dear, come back!

There is a letter from Beijing asking me to go, but I can't bear to go because I'm waiting for you. Come back soon, let's go together! Ziguang wrote a week ago saying that his mother was going to Shanghai and asked us to go to Nanjing to pick her up. I wrote back saying to have someone send her directly to Shanghai. She should be coming soon. I have already rented two comfortable rooms. You can imagine her disappointment and grief when she comes and doesn't see you! My dearest wife, have pity on your old mother! Have pity on me who is about to die! Hurry back! I will always be yours, you will always be mine. I will always wait for you until I die! For the sake of saving my life, you should ignore everything else and hurry back! You can go to Fifth Sister's house first. Your good tears book, June 8th, (Thank you)

A Scene of Man Eating Man 262

— Bin Fu

One Sunday afternoon after a sudden rain, it was the most crowded time in front of the Great World. Groups of men, women, old, and young were coming out from inside, and groups of men, women, old, and young were going in from outside. The road was filled with rickshaw pullers pulling empty carts and hoping for business.

"The patrol is coming!" Many rickshaws followed the pullers' legs and ran forward. An old man, dragging his weak legs, fell to the back, frequently looking back at the copper-pot hat pacing along behind him in a panic.

A 1933 Chevrolet car sped from the west, almost colliding with this fleeing rickshaw. Fortunately, it stopped abruptly. The old puller, concerned about the copper-pot hat behind him, let the car pass and continued to run forward, but the pale-faced man in the front of the car, wearing a silk short shirt and pants, suddenly jumped out of the carriage and pulled the rickshaw back with all his might. This strength was truly astonishing. The useless rickshaw puller almost fell backward with the cart.

"Chi ta, chi ta..." A palm extended from the rolled-up silk sleeves, emitting a crisp sound on a dry old face. At the same time, a crisp laugh also came from the depths of the Chevrolet car, but these two kinds of "crispness" seemed discordant.

This laughter was truly a great encouragement to the person with the rolled-up silk sleeves. He became even more valiant, and he twisted the puller's whole body even more fiercely. The puller dodged left and right. At first, he used the rickshaw as a shield, but later even the cart was overturned. Then he was defenseless and lay prostrate, only able to use his arms as protection.

The copper-pot hat arrived at this time. Under the double threat, the rickshaw puller became even more apprehensive. He hurriedly withdrew his hand that was touching the painful spot, stood up from his squatting position, collected his sorrowful face, and revealed his yellow-black teeth like a tame sheep, saying in a low voice, "I didn't do anything wrong..." But the copper-pot hat's attention was finally attracted by the car driver's滔滔 (滔滔: flowery, eloquent) narration. He narrated how this damned rickshaw puller violated the rules and almost frightened his X Mansion's fourth concubine. The copper-pot hat nodded repeatedly, glared fiercely at the rickshaw puller, and then shook out his diary and wrote down the rickshaw's number.

"Ah San, what's the matter?" A voice came from inside the car.

"It's alright, young mistress."

"We have to go, if there's anything, go back to the mansion and talk about it later."

"Yes, yes, young mistress!" The silk sleeves triumphantly returned to the car. The surrounding area of the car was already full of onlookers, and their gazes were all focused on the disheveled hair and cherry lips of the person. The car's horn sounded, and the people around slowly dispersed.

The copper-pot hat was "勒勒" (勒勒: a dialectal term for meticulously, painstakingly) prying open the rickshaw's certificate, and the rickshaw puller, with a mourning face, knelt on the ground and begged...

The car driver, Ah San, looked triumphantly at the rickshaw puller kneeling on the ground, turned his head and smiled at his young mistress, and started the car.

See! This is car driver and rickshaw puller, man eating man!

Shop Assistant Communication

Fiancee Commits Adultery 263

Editor-in-Chief,

I have a difficult matter, please guide me. My parents, several years ago, arranged a marriage for me; the other party is the daughter of a certain Yan from the same village. Now we have both become adults, and we should have been married long ago: but my economic situation is difficult, so we have not yet married. Who knew that in the past few years, she had a relationship with a certain Gong, and now she is several months pregnant. We had heard about this before, but we had no real evidence, so we did not negotiate. On a certain day of the month, Mr. Gong actually hired a lawyer and made a request to my father to cancel the engagement, so that they could fulfill their desire to live together. My father is honest by nature and agreed to let Mr. Gong compensate for the losses and cancel the engagement. Who knew that when the day came to pay the money, Mr. Gong actually insisted on reducing the amount of silver and forced me to write a receipt; my father was furious, and the matter was stopped in the middle. Litigation is bound to be involved in the future. I don't know what the legal point of view on this matter is? Please reply immediately, this please.

Sincerely, Fang Mengwei

Editor's note: Mr. Gong's adultery with the Yan woman is the crime of obstructing the family. Only the Yan woman's parents have the right to sue. Because Mr. Fang is not married to the Yan woman, he cannot exercise his husband's rights. However, since the Yan woman has committed adultery and is pregnant, the conditions for canceling the engagement have been established. Currently, Mr. Fang should file a lawsuit with the court to cancel the engagement based on this point, and he can also demand all the expenses previously used, and in addition, he can demand a sum of consolation money.

Simple Regulations for Soliciting Contemporary Calligraphy and Painting Manuscripts 264

1. This publication has specially opened a column to publish masterpieces of calligraphy and painting by famous contemporary writers in order to promote national essence and improve readers' appreciation interests.

2. All contemporary famous writers who wish to announce calligraphy and painting works are welcome to take photos and send them to this publication. It is especially welcome if they can briefly describe the writer's biography and style.

3. Modern works such as hall hangings and screen strips must be photographed, and other fan surfaces, foot pages, vertical hangings, etc., can be original or photographed as you please.

4. Modern works are best with good composition creation and elegant brushwork, otherwise they will not be accepted. However, excessively detailed and light works may be difficult to engrave and are also inconvenient to publish.

5. There are no fees for modern calligraphy and painting works.

6. If you want to return photos or works, please attach a registered postage stamp.

Fiction

The Life of Fifth Wife (Continuation 29) 265

— Ling He

27, Revenge (1)

This day was Minister Su's fifty-third birthday, and Fifth Wife was determined to celebrate it in a lively manner. It is said that some concubines wanted to celebrate the master's birthday in order to gain considerable benefits from the gifts, but Fifth Wife didn't seem to be doing it for that reason; perhaps she didn't care about those things.

Indeed, with a minister's connections, his circle was naturally very wide. Students and subordinates took this opportunity to show respect to their superiors and had to give gifts, and old relatives and distant relatives also had to give gifts in order to curry favor. They gave gifts last year, they give gifts again this year, and they will have to give gifts next year. The minister's birthday comes every year, so everyone has many opportunities to give gifts.

However, since they gave gifts and spent money, it was only right to have a celebratory meal. Therefore, Wu Gui really put in a lot of effort this time. However, according to Fifth Wife's idea, it would be best to eat Western food, which would be more civilized, but Wu Gui stubbornly insisted on using top-quality Cantonese cuisine. In the end, Fifth Wife let Wu Gui have his way, thinking that he had been loyal all his life, so why not give him a little face on this small matter?

Fifth Wife accompanied Minister Su in mingling with the guests, and then invited Manager Gu to come into the bedroom together. They saw He Xiang directing several maids to set up a table of exquisite wine and dishes. Manager Gu couldn't help but laugh loudly, saying, "So, I have to accompany the birthday star here to eat some special delicacies?"

"Of course, how could Minister Gu be treated like an ordinary guest?" Fifth Wife replied with a smile. Minister Su had nothing to say, just laughing all the time.

Tonight, Fifth Wife was truly virtuous. In addition to diligently offering wine, she also placed the most precious dishes in front of Minister Su, but she also treated Manager Gu with the same great hospitality. Of course, she also drank several glasses herself, until the whites of her eyes were filled with red veins. Soon, she stood up and said to the two of them with a solemn smile...

"Originally, today is the old man's birthday, and logically I should let the old man be as happy as possible. However, there is one thing that must be resolved tonight. Fortunately, Minister Gu is not an outsider, so let you two talk about this letter."

As she spoke, she took out a letter from her pocket. Su Gengyun was naturally surprised and suspicious, but he immediately took out the letter and read it word by word.

"My dear Willow Silk…

Recently, I have been busy translating the secret documents of the old thief and Gu, and because there are too many of them, I have been busy for several nights in a row. These include the edict of the XX country's special envoy to China, Minister of Political Affairs, and documents from the General Staff Headquarters. The most important of these are the designated military conference plan and the procedures for merging the countries. The documents related to Gu include progress reports, a list of entertainment expenses from the XX country's political affairs office in China, the balance of the old thief's international activity funds stored in the Bank of Taiwan, and rebates on loans for certain items, etc. This list of passbooks totals more than 57 million yuan. Now, my love, it is best to tell the old thief that if he can agree to our conditions, then the old thief's letters and drafts can be returned, but Gu's financial decree and lists, etc., can be used as evidence. My love, if the old thief dares to sell the country, wouldn't he also sell the old thief?

Autumn wind is harsh, take care of yourself.

Yours, Wenbin."
